Title: Manage Driver Documents
URL: https://helpdesk.uffizio.com/knowledge/manage-driver-documents

Manage Driver Documents
Manage all of the driver documents in one place and organize important information like training records, certifications, and licenses. This can help ensure that only qualified and properly trained drivers operate vehicles and help comply with regulations. When compared to manual record-keeping, having all driver documents in a digital format can also save time and resources.
To Get Started
Log in to your account.
Go to
Settings > General > Driver.
Double-click on the driver record for which you want to upload the Driver Documents.
To Upload Driver Documents
Navigate to the Documents Tab
Click on
Document ➕.
Select the appropriate
Document Type
for the document you intend to upload from the dropdown list.
Enter
Document Name.
Upload the Document
from your system.
Choose the appropriate
Issue Date
by utilizing the date picker provided.
Choose the
Expiry Date
using the date picker provided.
You can download the document by clicking on the
Download
icon.
To set a reminder for your document's expiry date, simply click on the
Add Reminder
icon, which will help you ensure timely renewal.
Add
Reminder Name
for your reference.
Select the
Reminder Type
from the dropdown.
Notify Before (X) Days:
Indicate the number of days in advance you wish to receive the reminder.
Choose your preferred method of receiving reminders from the
Remind Using
field.
Notification:
Choose the appropriate users from the dropdown list under the
"Notify To"
section to receive notifications.
SMS:
Add the mobile number in the provided text box on which you want to send the reminder. Use a comma (,) as a separator if you are adding multiple mobile numbers.
Email:
Add the email address to which you want to send the reminder. Use comma (,) as a separator if you are adding multiple email addresses.
The
Email Configuration
or
SMS Configuration
is required in order to receive Email or SMS for reminder.
You can also
Delete
the document by clicking on the delete
icon.
Click on
Save 💾
button.

Driver Leave

Go to
Settings > General > Driver Leave
Once you click on Driver leave, you will find list of all the leave requests
In
Leave Status
you will find the status of the leave, if the leave is approved Declined or Pending.
Please Note :
In Leave Status,
means the leave has beed accepted,
means the leave has been rejected,
means no action has been peformed for the requested leave.
click on the
Action icon to Approve or Decline the leave.

Action
Drop-down select from Approved or Declined.

Declined
from the Action dropdown, you will find a reason box, where you can mention the reson for declining the leave.

The Changes will also be reflected in the Driver mobile application.

================================================================================

Title: Alerts Description
URL: https://helpdesk.uffizio.com/knowledge/alerts-description

Alerts Description
This article offers a comprehensive overview of the various alerts available on the platform. Below, you will find detailed descriptions of each alert.
General Alerts
911:
It is a device-specific alert triggered by the 911 emergency telephone number. Notification can be received as an action, whenever the alert is triggered.
AC Misuse:
AC Misuse alert is triggered when the AC is in use during the idling of the vehicle for more than defined time. As an action when the alert is triggered, the notification can be received or you can also immobilize the vehicle. This is a configuration specific alert.
Address Overstay:
Address Overstay alert is triggered when the vehicle stays in the radius of selected addresses for more than the defined time. As an action when the alert is triggered, the notification can be received or you can also immobilize the vehicle.
Air Condition:
AC alert can be configured to receive alerts whenever the AC is turned ON or OFF. Notification can be received as an action, whenever the alert is triggered.
Alcohol Level Violation:
This alert will be triggered whenever the alcohol level crosses the threshold defined while configuring the sensor. Notification can be received or the vehicle can be immobilized as an action, whenever the alert is triggered.
Alcohol Sensor:
Alcohol Sensor alert will be triggered when the sensor is disconnected. This is a device specific alert and the notification can be received as an action whenever the alert is generated.
Authorized Break:
The alert will be triggered when the vehicle fails to take the minimum required break within the set duration time. Notification can be received as an action, whenever the alert is triggered to take specific break time.
Base Location Delay:
Once the object starts from the base location source, if it doesn't reach end point within the specified duration in hours. A notification action can be received whenever the alert is triggered.
Base delay Visit:
Once the object departs from the base location source and fails to reach another designated point within the specified duration in hours, an alert will be triggered. Notifications can be received whenever the alert is triggered.
Battery:
The battery alert will be triggered whenever the battery is plugged or unplugged. Notification can be received as an action, whenever the alert is triggered.
Battery Threshold:
This alert is triggered when the battery voltage drops below a configured threshold. It notifies the user that "Battery Maintenance Required" via SMS, email, or API as configured.
Beacon:
Beacon alert will be triggered whenever the beacon is connected or disconnected. Notification can be received as an action, whenever the alert is triggered.
BLE Battery Sensor:
This alert is a device specific alert. The alert will be triggered whenever the battery is about to discharge and the notification can be received as an action.
BLE Missing:
The BLE Missing alert is triggered when the bluetooth is not connected. This is a device specific alert and a notification can be received as an action whenever the alert is triggered.
BLE Tamper:
The alert will be triggered when the bluetooth is tampered. It is a device specific alert and whenever an alert is triggered, a notification can be received as an action.
BLE Temperature Sensor:
This is a device specific alert and is triggered whenever the sensor is connected. Notification can be received as an action, whenever the alert is triggered.
Boot:
Boot alert can be configured to receive alerts whenever the boot's switch is turned ON or OFF. Notification can be received as an action, whenever the alert is triggered.
Charger:
Charger alert will be triggered whenever the charger is connected or disconnected. Notification can be received as an action, whenever the alert is triggered.
Checkpoint halt violation:
This is a job related alert. If the vehicle takes a halt for more than the time period defined for halt on checkpoints while configuring the job, then this alert will be triggered. Notification can be received as an action, whenever the alert is triggered.
Collision alarm:
This is an ADAS event specific and device specific alert. The collision alarm alert will trigger an alarm in case there is a possibility of an accident. Notification can be received as an action, whenever the alert is triggered.
Convoy violation:
This is alert is triggered when the convoy vehicle moves out of the tolerance set while configuring the job, for more than the time period defined. Notification can be received as an action, whenever the alert is triggered.
Crash detection:
The crash detection alert is triggered when the vehicle has met with an accident. This is an event specific and device specific alert. Notification can be received as an action, whenever the alert is triggered.
Custom:
This is a custom Digital Alert. The user needs to select Custom from the dropdown menu in Connected Sensor list while configuring the Object. Notification can be received as an action, whenever the alert is triggered.
Depart from Address:
This alert will be triggered whenever the vehicle enters and comes out of all the selected addresses. Notification can be received as an action, whenever the alert is triggered.
Device low battery:
This alert can be set when the user wants to receive a notification when the device battery is low. Notification can be received as an action, whenever the alert is triggered.
The alert can be set based on either of the following parameters:
Event:
When the user configures an alert based on event then the alert will be generated whenever the device has low battery.
Custom:
The alert will be generated whenever the device battery is lower than the battery percentage you set. To avoid false values due to fluctuations, you need to set a time period for which the battery percentage remains constant and user should receive the alert.
Diagnostic trouble codes:
This alert is generated on the basis of DTC error codes. It works on vehicle CAN or OBD ports. Notification can be received as an action, whenever the alert is triggered.
Disassemble:
The alert is generated whenever the device is disassembled. This is a device specific alert and notification can be received as an action, whenever the alert is triggered.
District:
The alert is generated whenever the district is changed by the vehicle. This alert depends on address. Notification can be received as an action, whenever the alert is triggered.
Door:
Door alert can be configured to receive alerts whenever the door is opened or closed. Notification can be received as an action, whenever the alert is triggered.
Driver drunk:
This alert is generated when the driver is drunk. This alert depends on the sensor configuration done by the user. Notification can be received as an action, whenever the alert is triggered.
Driver Face-ID Authentication:
The Driver Face-ID Authentication alert verifies driver identity using facial recognition when the vehicle ignition is turned on. A snapshot is taken and compared with stored Face-ID records. If the face matches, an "Authorized Driver" alert is generated; otherwise, an "Unauthorized Driver" alert is generated. The alert includes a snapshot link for verification.
Driver Swipe Missing:
This alert is triggered when a journey begins without the driver's card being scanned at the start of the trip. The alert checks within a set duration (default 120 seconds) and notifies if the card is not detected.
Drop alarm:
This is a device specific alert (personal trackers) and the alert is generated when the device is dropped.
Emergency Lights:
This alert is triggered when the emergency lights' status changes (On/Off). It functions like the ignition alert and supports SMS, email, and API notifications. The alert can be configured to consider On, Off, or both statuses.
Engine:
Engine alert can be configured to receive alerts whenever the engine starts or stops. Notification can be received as an action, whenever the alert is triggered.
Engine Temperature:
This alert is triggered when the engine temperature exceeds a user-specified threshold (1°C to 130°C). The alert provides a message indicating that the engine temperature has reached its set threshold, notifying users promptly.
Enter in Geofence:
This alert is generated whenever the vehicle enters in the selected geofences. This alert will only be applicable for the geofences whose category is selected as area while configuring the geofence.
External low battery protection:
This alert is generated when the external battery is low. Notification can be received as an action, whenever the alert is triggered.
Eye sensor device low battery:
This alert can be set when the user wants to receive a notification when the eye sensor device battery is low. This is a device specific alert and notification can be received as an action, whenever the alert is triggered.
The alert can be set based on either of the following parameters:
Event:
When the user configures an alert based on event then the alert will be generated whenever the eye sensor device has low battery.
Custom:
The alert will be generated whenever the eye sensor device battery is lower than the battery percentage you set. To avoid false values due to fluctuations, you need to set a time period for which the battery percentage remains constant and user should receive the alert.
Eye sensor humidity:
This alert whenever the humididty is in defined values. This is a  device specific alert and a notification can be received as a action whenever the alert is triggered.
Eye sensor idle:
The alert is triggered whenever the Eye sensor is in Idling greater than the defined time period, which means the Ignition is ON but the Eye sensor is in idling. This is a  device specific alert and a notification can be received as a action whenever the alert is triggered.
Eye sensor magentic field:
This alert is triggered whenever there is a magnetic field detected by the Eye sensor. This alert is majorly used for construction site. It is a  device specific alert and a notification can be received as a action whenever the alert is triggered.
Eye sensor movement:
This alert is triggered whenever there is some movement of Eye sensor detected or not detected. This is a device specific alert and a notification can be received as a action whenever the alert is triggered.
Eye sensor temperature:
This alert is triggered whenever the temperature is in defined values. It is a  device specific alert and a notification can be received as a action whenever the alert is triggered.
Fall Detection:
This alert is triggered when the person falls down. It is a device specific alert for the personal trackers and a notification can be received as a action whenever the alert is triggered.
Fence Overstay:
The fence overstay alert is for the times when the vehicle stays in the selected geofence for more than time user defines in value. Only running vehicles will be considered for this alert. In order to consider the vehicles in stoppage, the box needs to be checked. As an action when the alert is triggered, the notification can be received or you can also immobilize the vehicle.
Free Wheeling:
This alert is triggered when a vehicle is in motion with the accelerator pedal in a neutral position or low RPM (≤ 600) for more than 2 minutes. It helps detect risky downhill driving practices that can lead to vehicle breakdowns.
Fuel:
This alert is triggered when the fuel is less than the liters defined as value. A notification can be received as a action whenever the alert is triggered.
Fuel Data Interruption:
When the fuel hardware is damaged or interrupted, the alert will be triggered. Whenever the voltage value is less than the defined value for more than the defined time period, it will be considered as damaged/interrupted. A notification can be received as a action whenever the alert is triggered.
Fuel Impurity:
This alert will be triggered whenever there is some impurity found in fuel like water, etc. The alert is fuel sensor specific and a notification can be received as a action whenever the alert is triggered.
Fuel Pilferage:
This alert is triggered in case of theft. The alert is based on the threshold set as drain difference in fuel calibration. A notification can be received as a action whenever the alert is triggered.
Fuel Refill:
This alert is triggered in case of refill. The alert is based on the threshold set as fill difference in fuel calibration. A notification can be received as a action whenever the alert is triggered.
Fuel Sensor Disconnect:
This alert is triggered when the fuel sensor gets disconnected based on the fuel calibration settings. It notifies users with a message to check the sensor connection and supports SMS, email, and API notifications.
Fuel Sensor Error:
This alert is triggered based on specific error codes from the fuel sensor data, indicating issues like faulty sensors, incorrect calibration, or water in the fuel tank. It generates notifications via SMS, email, or API as per configuration.
Fuel Sensor Shielded:
This alert is triggered when a fuel sensor is covered or tampered with. It monitors specific ports and generates notifications if tampering is detected, supporting SMS, email, and API notifications.
G-Sensor:
This alert will be triggered when there is some violation in the Gravity sensor. It is a device specific alert and a notification can be received as an action whenever the alert is triggered.
Geofence Overcrowding:
This alert will be triggered when the number of vehicles exceeds the limit set in the selected geofence area. A notification action can be received whenever the alert is triggered.
GPS Geofence:
This alert will be triggered when a vehicle enters or exits the geofence area. It is device-specific, as the geofence list has been added to the device.
It is a device specific alert and a notification can be received as an action whenever the alert is triggered.
GPS Towing:
This alert is triggered when a vehicle is towed. It is a device specific alert and a notification can be received as an action whenever the alert is triggered.
GSM Signal Loss:
This alert is triggered when the GSM signal is lost due to network issues, prompting the device to send an event. It is a device specific alert and a notification can be received as an action whenever the alert is triggered.
Harsh Acceleration:
This alert can be triggered in two ways:
Event:
In the event-based triggering, it relies on the magnitude received from the device, with custom considerations for magnitude if specified.
Custom:
in the custom-based triggering, it's only dependent on the magnitude received from the device. A notification action can be received whenever the alert is triggered.
Harsh Braking:
In the event-based triggering, it relies on the magnitude received from the device, with custom considerations for magnitude if specified, and if it exceeds the set speed limit. In the custom-based triggering, it's only dependent on the magnitude received from the device and if it exceeds the set speed limit. A notification action can be received whenever the alert is triggered.
Harsh Cornering:
This alert is activated when a vehicle makes sharp turns while driving. It is a device specific and a notification can be received as an action whenever the alert is triggered.
Help:
This alert, specific to personal trackers, allows for starting, cancelling, or both actions. It is a device specific alert and a notification can be received as an action whenever the alert is triggered.
Humidity:
The alert is triggered when the humidity sensor detects humidity levels beyond the configured range. A notification action can be received whenever the alert is triggered.
Idle:
The alert will triggered when the vehicle remains idle for a duration exceeding the specified time period. A notification action can be received whenever the alert is triggered.
Ignition/ACC:
The alert activates when the ignition is turned on, off, or both. A notification action can be received whenever the alert is triggered.
Immobilize:
The alert is triggered when the immbolize is on, off, or both. A notification action can be received whenever the alert is triggered.
Immobilize Movement:
The alert is triggered when the vehicle moves above the set speed limit despite being immobilized. A notification action can be received whenever the alert is triggered.
Inactive:
The alert is triggered when the vehicle status changes to inactive. A notification action can be received whenever the alert is triggered.
Incorrect Ignition:
The alert is triggered when the vehicle is moving at the specified speed for a duration longer than the defined time period while the ignition is off. A notification action can be received whenever the alert is triggered.
Jamming:
The alert is activated when the GPS signal is shown off due to a jammer. It is device specific alert and a notification can be received as an action whenever the alert is triggered.
Job:
The alert triggers when a job is created for both the company and the driver. A notification action can be received whenever the alert is triggered.
Job Arrival:
The alert triggers when the vehicle arrives at the last point of the job early, delay, or both than the scheduled arrival time. A notification action can be received whenever the alert is triggered.
Job Departure:
The alert triggers when the vehicle arrives at the first point of the job early, delay, or both than the scheduled departure time. A notification action can be received whenever the alert is triggered.
Job Route Deviation:
The alert is triggered when the vehicle deviates from the predefined route, either based on distance(m) or duration(min). A notification action can be received whenever the alert is triggered.
Job Status:
The alert is triggered when a job starts or ends. A notification action can be received whenever the alert is triggered.
Job Unauthorized Halt:
The alert is triggered when the vehicle remains stationary/ take halt beyond defined checkpoints for a specified duration. A notification action can be received whenever the alert is triggered.
Late Start:
This alert is triggered if a vehicle does not turn on its ignition within a specified time window each day. Users can configure the start time and a buffer duration (5 to 60 minutes). Notifications are sent via SMS, email, or API when the vehicle fails to start on time.
Light Alarm:
It is device specific link.
Location:
The alert will triggered when Location will be sent as an alert based on the schedule selected (Single/ Multiple). A notification action can be received whenever the alert is triggered.
Man down:
This is a device specific alert (personal trackers) and the alert is generated when the man fallen down.
Moving:
The alert activates when the vehicle is in the movement with speed. A notification action can be received whenever the alert is triggered when moving is on, off or both.
Night Driving:
The alert is activated when a vehicle moves during night-time within a specific duration either in an authorized or unauthorized area. A notification action can be recieved whenever the alert is triggered.
Nonstop Drive:
The alett is activated when a vehicle moves non stop without taking any stoppage based on duration or distance. A notification action can be recieved whenever the alert is triggered.
Off Route:
The alert is activated when a vehicle deviates from the predefined route format. A notification action can be received whenever the alert is triggered.
Out Of Geofence:
The alert is activated when a vehicle moves out of specific geofence area. A notification action can be recieved whenever the alerts is triggered.
Over Speed:
The alert is activated when a vehicle exceeds the speed limit for a specified duration of time. A notification action can be recieved whenever the alerts is triggered.
OverStay:
The alert is activated when a vehicle exceeds the speed limit for a specified duration of time. A notification action can be recieved whenever the alerts is triggered.
Overtime Drive:
The alert will triggered when it has been configured based on distance and duration. A notification action can be received whenever the alert is triggered.
Overweight:
It's a weight sensor, the alert get activated when a specific vehicle exceeds its weight capacity. A notification alert can be recieved whenever the alert is triggered.
Passed Address:
The alert activates when a vehicle passes through its designated POI address. A notification alert can be recieved whenever the alert is triggered.
Passenger Seat:
This digital port configured by a sensor is used to detect whether someone is seated beside it or not. A notification alert can be recieved whenever the alert is triggered.
Power:
The alert is triggered when there is a disruption in the device's power port, typically caused by someone cutting the wire. This sensor-based alert indicates a disconnect or connect or always event. Notifications can be received whenever the alert is triggered.
Power off:
It is a device specific alert. The alert is sent from device event itself. Notifications can be received whenever the alert is triggered.
Proximity Violation:
This alert is specific to the device and is activated when a vehicle approaches a designated object, based on sensor-based configuration. Notifications can be received whenever the alert is triggered.
Reached Address:
The alert is triggered when a vehicle arrives at a specific POI address. A notification alert can be recieved whenever the alert is triggered.
Reverse:
The alert is activated when a vehicle reverses, triggering an alert in case of any incidents. A notification alert can be recieved whenever the alert is triggered.
RFID:
The alert is activated when a vehicle is authorized or unauthorized or both via RFID detection. A notification alert can be recieved whenever the alert is triggered.
Seat Belt:
The alert is digital and monitors whether the driver is wearing a seatbelt or not. A notification alert can be recieved whenever the alert is triggered.
Sharp Left Turn:
The alert is triggered when a vehicle makes a sharp left turn. It is a device-specific event. A notification alert can be recieved whenever the alert is triggered.
Sharp Right Turn:
The alert is triggered when a vehicle makes a sharp right turn. It is a device-specific event. A notification alert can be recieved whenever the alert is triggered.
Ship Engine 3:
The alert is a digital port configured for ships. It is a sensor-based configuration that detects when the engine starts or stops. The alert can be triggered based on the start, stop, or both events. A notification alert can be recieved whenever the alert is triggered.
Sim Change:
The alert is triggered when the SIM card is changed in the device. It is a device-specific alert. A notification alert can be recieved whenever the alert is triggered.
SOS:
The alert is triggered when a panic alert is generated. It is configurable through sensors. A notification alert can be recieved whenever the alert is triggered.
Speedometer Tampering:
The alert is triggered when there is tampering with the speedometer, indicating whether it's on, off, or both. A notification alert can be recieved whenever the alert is triggered.
State Border Crossing:
The alert is triggered when a vehicle crosses the state border, prompting an address alert. A notification alert can be recieved whenever the alert is triggered.
Stay Away from Zone:
The alert is triggered when a vehicle approaches a geofence area where it is restricted from entering. A notification alert can be recieved before reaching the geofence. whenever the alert is triggered.
Stay in Zone:
The alert is triggered when a vehicle exits a designated geofence area where it is required to remain. A notification alert can be recieved before leaving the geofence. whenever the alert is triggered.
Sweeper:
It is a digital port alert indicating the status of the sweeper machine, whether it is on or off. A notification alert can be recieved whenever the alert is triggered.
System 3.5:
It is a customer specific alert.
Tamper:
The alert is triggered in case of GPS tampering, signaling if the device enclosure has been on or off or both with fraudulently.
Tank Lid:
The alert is activated by a digital sensor indicating when the tank lid is opened or closed. A notification alert can be recieved whenever the alert is triggered.
Temperature:
The alert triggers when the temperature exceeds the value set limit. A notification alert can be recieved whenever the alert is triggered.
Tow:
The alert is triggered when the vehicle is towed with the ignition off. This alert is based on device logic. A notification alert can be recieved whenever the alert is triggered.
Travel Distance:
The alert is triggered when the vehicle covers a specific distance limit. A notification alert can be recieved whenever the alert is triggered.
Underweight:
It's a weight sensor, the alert get activated when a specific vehicle falls below its weight capacity. A notification alert can be recieved whenever the alert is triggered.
Vehicle Low Battery:
The alert is triggered by the internal battery, when the battery level drops below a certain threshold, an alert is generated. A notification alert can be recieved whenever the alert is triggered.
Vibration:
The alert is triggered when the vehicle experiences vibrations, such as impacts or collisions, which are event-specific. A notification alert can be recieved whenever the alert is triggered.
Zone OverSpeeding:
The alert is triggered when the vehicle exceeds the set speed limit within a geofenced area of particular zone, indicating zone overspeeding. A notification alert can be recieved whenever the alert is triggered.
ELOCK
ELock Motor Fault:
This alert is triggered when a fault is detected in the ELock motor mechanism, indicating a malfunction or operational failure that requires immediate attention.
ELock Open Back Cap:
This alert is triggered when the back cap of the ELock is opened, indicating potential tampering or unauthorized access that requires immediate attention.
ELock State:
This alert is triggered when the ELock remains in a specific state (e.g., Locked or Unlocked) for a duration exceeding the configured threshold. This helps identify prolonged inactivity or potential issues requiring immediate attention.
ELock Status:
The alert is trigerred for the elock lock or unlock action, or for both events based on the alert configuration. Users have the option to set conditions for generating alerts, either while the vehicle is in operation or for all instances.
ELock Steel String Cut:
This alert is triggered when the steel string of the ELock is cut or tampered with, indicating a potential security breach that requires immediate action.
ELock Unauthorized RFID:
This alert is triggered when an unauthorized RFID tag attempts to access or operate the ELock, indicating a potential security threat or unauthorized access attempt.
ELock Wrong Password:
This alert is triggered when a password entered into the ELock system is wrong or does not match the defined system password, indicating either user error or a potential unauthorized access attempt.
Sublock Battery Status Low:
This alert is triggered when the sublock's battery level falls below a specified threshold and the device send this event.
Sublock Motor Lock Status:
This alert refers to the current operational state of the sublock motor, indicating whether the motor is locked or unlocked. The alert is trigerred for the elock lock or unlock action, or for both events based on the alert configuration.
Sublock Rope Inserted:
This alert is triggered when the rope is inserted into the sublock mechanism. It helps monitor the proper operation of the locking system and ensures that the rope is correctly placed for securing the object or asset.
Sublock Rope Remove:
This alert is triggered when the rope is removed from the sublock mechanism. It indicates potential tampering or an action that may require attention to ensure the security of the locked asset.
DMS
Calibration Fail:
This alert is triggered when the device sends a Calibration Fail event due to calibration issues, such as camera misalignment, failure to detect the driver’s face or eyes, or technical problems like poor lighting. It indicates that the video device is not functioning properly and may need recalibration for accurate driver monitoring.
Distraction:
This alert is triggered when the DMS detects signs of driver distraction, such as looking away from the road, excessive head movement, or other behaviors indicating a lack of focus.
Driver On Call:
This alert is triggered when the DMS detects that the driver is actively engaged in a phone call while driving or during their shift. This status helps monitor driver activity and ensure compliance with regulations regarding driving while on the phone.
Eye Closed:
This alert is triggered by the DMS when it detects that the driver’s eyes are closed for a certain duration, which may indicate drowsiness.
Fatigue Driving:
This alert is triggered when the DMS detects signs of driver fatigue, such as prolonged eye closure, yawning, or a lack of head movement.
Look Down:
This alert is triggered when the DMS detects that the driver is looking down for an extended period, which may indicate distraction or engagement in activities like using a mobile device.
Missing Face:
This alert is triggered when the DMS detects that the driver's face is not visible to the camera, either due to the driver turning away, leaning, or any obstruction.
Monitoring Shelter:
This alert is triggered when the DMS detects that the vehicle is within a sheltered or obstructed environment, such as a covered area, where the camera or sensors may not be able to effectively monitor the driver.
Smoking:
This alert is triggered when the DMS detects signs of smoking, such as visible smoke or the driver’s actions consistent with smoking behavior.
Yawn:
This alert is triggered when the DMS detects that the driver is yawning, which can be a sign of fatigue or drowsiness.
ADAS
Forward Collision Warning:
This alert is triggered by the Advanced Driver Assistance System (ADAS) when it detects a potential risk of a forward collision with another vehicle or obstacle.
Headway Monitor Warning:
This alert is triggered by the ADAS when it detects that the vehicle is following too closely behind another vehicle, based on the set headway distance or safe following distance. The warning notifies the driver to increase the distance from the vehicle ahead, preventing rear-end collisions and enhancing safety.
Lane Departure Warning:
This alert is triggered by the ADAS when the vehicle unintentionally drifts out of its lane without signaling. The system notifies the driver to correct their steering and return to the lane.
Pedestrian in Danger Zone:
This alert is triggered by the ADAS when it detects a pedestrian in or near the vehicle’s path, indicating a potential collision risk.
Traffic Sign Recognition Warning:
This alert is triggered by the ADAS when it detects traffic signs, such as speed limits or stop signs, and warns the driver if they are approaching or violating a traffic regulation.
Urban Forward Collision Warning:
This alert is triggered by the ADAS when it detects potential collisions with objects or vehicles in urban environments, such as pedestrians, cyclists, or other vehicles, while the vehicle is driving at low speeds.
Base Location
Base Unauthorized Movement:
This alert is triggered when a vehicle is detected moving outside its designated base location and exceeds the specified distance threshold.
Base Unauthorized Overstay:
This alert is triggered when a vehicle is stays outside the designated base location beyond the allowed time or exceeds the defined duration limit.
RPM
RPM High:
This alert is triggered when the engine RPM exceeds a predefined upper threshold set in the calibration for a specified duration. It indicates potential issues such as aggressive driving, speeding, or excessive engine load.
RPM Idling:
This alert notifies when a vehicle remains idle within the configured RPM calibraion range for an extended period, leading to potential fuel wastage, increased emissions, and unnecessary engine wear.
RPM Low:
This alert is triggered when the engine RPM falls below a predefined lower threshold in calibration for a specified duration. It may signal issues such as engine stalling, poor fuel efficiency, or insufficient power.
TPMS
Tire Pressure:
The alert is triggered when the tire pressure reaches either the minimum or maximum threshold, or in both scenarios, based on the events received from the device and the configured alert settings.
Tire Temperature:
The alert is trigerred when the tire temperature falls outside of the designated thresholds, whether it be too low or too high, based on the events reported by the device and the specified alert configurations.

Title: Add an Alert for the Object
URL: https://helpdesk.uffizio.com/knowledge/add-an-alert-for-the-object

Add an Alert for the Object
An
Alert
serves as a notification that is activated in response to a specific event or condition, such as when a vehicle exceeds the established speed limit or a driver surpasses their allotted service hours. Alerts can be set up to notify fleet managers or designated personnel through various channels, such as email and text, facilitating prompt action on potential issues and ensuring regulatory compliance.
Watch :
How to create alert for object.
To Get Started
Log in to your account.
Go to
Settings > General > Alert.
Upon clicking on
Alert
, users will be directed to the alert overview screen, where they can view and manage all existing alerts.
Click on the ➕ button on the taskbar. A new window will open.
Choose the appropriate
Company
and
Branch
from the dropdown menu for which you would like to configure the alert.
To select vehicles for sending alerts, choose from
Object, Object Type, or Object Group
in the
Based On
field. Based on your selection, a list of relevant objects will appear in the
Object
field.
Object:
If you want to select different objects, then select Object.
Choose the desired
Object
from the dropdown list for which you wish to send alerts.
Object group:
If you want to add an alert to a certain group of objects, then select object group.
Select
Object Group
from the drop-down list if you want to configure alerts for a specific group of objects. The corresponding objects will be displayed in the Object drop-down menu, allowing you to choose the objects according to your requirement.
Object Group
created under the same Company and Branch will appear in the drop-down menu. Learn how to create
Object Group.
Object type:
If you want to add an alert based on the type of object, then select object type.
Choose the
Object Type
from the dropdown list for which you wish to set up an alert. The corresponding objects will be displayed in the Object drop-down menu, allowing you to choose the objects according to your requirement.
Assign a descriptive
Alert Name
that reflects the purpose of the alert you are configuring for easy identification.
Choose the appropriate
Alert Type
from the dropdown list for the alert you wish to configure.
Choose the appropriate
Value
based on the selected alert type. For instance, if you wish to receive an alert when the air conditioning system is activated, select "start."
The options available in the
Value
field will differ depending on the selected Alert Type, as each alert is governed by unique conditions that define its specific criteria.
The
Text
field will present the default content intended as the heading of the alert. You have the option to customize this text to ensure it effectively communicates the purpose of the alert.
Set the validity of when you want the alert to be generated.
Everyday:
If you want the alerts to be generated on a daily basis, then you can select every day.
Valid Time From:
Determine the specific start and end times during which you would like the alerts to be generated.
Select the
Timezone
that corresponds to your location, as this will determine when the alerts are generated.
Custom:
If you want to generate alerts on some particular days, then you can select custom.
Week Days:
Choose the specific days of the week on which you would like the alert to be generated.
Valid Time From:
Determine the specific time frame during which you would like the alert to be triggered.
Time zone:
Select the preferred time zone when you want to receive the alerts.
Choose the level of
Severity
for the alert from the dropdown menu.
Action:
Choose your preferred method for sending alerts.
SMS:
Add the mobile number in the provided text box on which you want to send the alerts. Use a comma (,) as a separator if you are adding multiple mobile numbers.
Please Note:
SMS configuration
is necessary.
Email:
Add the email address to which you want to send the alerts. Use a comma (,) as a separator if you are adding multiple email addresses.
Click on
Verify Email
to verify the entered email addresses.
Please Note:
Email configuration
is necessary.
When you click on
Verify Email,
a verification email will be sent to the addresses you provided. Please check your inbox and confirm the email to begin receiving future emails for alerts.
Notification:
To notify subusers with alerts, select Notification.
Choose the
Users
from the dropdown list who should receive the notification.
You may also choose a specific
Notification sound
for each alert to enhance your experience.
Social Media API:
To notify subusers with alerts through the configured Social Media API, select this option.
Choose the appropriate
Gateway
from the drop-down list.
Enter the
Recipient's phone number
to which the alerts will be sent. Use a comma (,) as a separator if you are adding multiple email addresses.
Please Note:
Social Media API
configuration is necessary to use the option.
Save the configuration by clicking on the
Save 💾
icon.
To add an alert from the mobile application, click
here
.
To download alert details from the mobile application, click
here
.

Title: Add Reminder Rule
URL: https://helpdesk.uffizio.com/knowledge/reminder-rule

Add Reminder Rule
A reminder rule is a feature that allows users to set up reminders for maintenance and renewal activities of the assets. Reminders can be set up for vehicle maintenance, driver license renewal, insurance renewal, and more.
Users have the ability to create personalized reminder rules according to their unique requirements and can specify their desired timings for these reminders.
Reminders can be categorized into three distinct types: Time-based Reminders, Distance-based Reminders, and Work Hour-based Reminders.
Time-based Reminders
are the reminders that are set on the basis of time period. For example, a user can set a reminder rule to notify them when a state permit is due for renewal every year.
Distance-based Reminders
are the reminders that are set on the basis of distance travelled. For example, a user can set a reminder to notify them when a vehicle is due for a service after travelling every 1500 kilometers.
Work Hour-based Reminders
are the reminders that are set on the basis of engine hours. For example, a user can set a reminder to notify them when an object is due for an oil change after every 200 engine hours.
Please Note:
Reminder Rule is included only in
Standard
and
Premium
versions of the platform.
Watch :
How to configure Reminder.
To Get Started
Log in to your account.
Go to
Settings > General > Reminder Rule.
To Set Reminder
Click on the
➕
button on the taskbar.
Choose the
Reseller
and
Company
from the drop-down menu.
Please provide a
Name
for the
Reminder
Rule
to help you easily identify it later.
You can
Add a New Reminder Type
or
Select
the existing
Reminder Type
from the dropdown list. The new reminder type created will get added under others.
Select the
S
chedule
type for the reminder: Recurring or One Time.
Remind every (x) month:
Specify the number of months in this
field to receive reminders on a monthly basis.
Notify Before (x) Days:
To receive a notification several days prior to the end of the month, please enter the desired number of days in this field.
Every (x) Distance:
Please specify the distance at which you would like to receive a notification when your vehicle reaches a specified number of kilometers.
Notify Before Every (x) Distance:
Please specify the distance at which you would like to be notified prior to your vehicle reaching the designated kilometer mark.
Every (x) Engine Hour:
Please specify the preferred time in hours to receive notifications when your vehicle reaches a specified number of engine hours.
Notify Before Every (x) Engine Hour:
Please specify the number of hours at which you would like to be notified prior to your vehicle reaches the desired engine hour.
Select the method you want to get reminded from the
Remind Using
field.
Notification:
Select Notification to notify subusers.
Notify To:
Select users from the dropdown list to whom you want to send reminder notifications.
SMS:
Add the mobile number in the provided text box on which you want to send the reminder. Use a comma (,) as a separator if you are adding multiple mobile numbers.
Please Note:
SMS configuration
is necessary.
Email:

Title: Pair Device
URL: https://helpdesk.uffizio.com/knowledge/pair-device

Pair Device
Pair Device is a feature in the application that works on a parent-child relationship of GPS devices.
The parent-child arrangement will assist in generating condition warnings based on data from both devices. This way, the user will receive an alert only when all the connected devices are inactive at the same time.
Please Note:
The Pair Device module is included only in the
Standard
and
Premium
versions of the platform.
To Get Started
Login to your account.
Go to
Settings > General > Pair Device.
When you click on
Pair Device
, you will be taken to the
Pair Device Overview
page, where you can review all your paired device records.
To Pair the Devices
Click on the ➕ button on the taskbar.
Select the
Reseller
and
Company
under which you want to pair the devices from the drop-down menu.
Select the
Primary Object
from the drop-down list.
Select the
Secondary Object
from the drop-down list.
Multiple secondary objects can be selected from the list to pair with a single primary object.
Click on the
Save 💾 icon
to pair the devices.
Please Note:
You need to set the Inactive alert only on the Primary Object. You will receive the Inactive alert only when all the devices that are paired will go Inactive at the same time.
To Download Multiple Records
You can use the
Export
button (at the bottom of the page) to download the paired device data in XLS format.

Smart Trip

This feature can be particularly useful for businesses that need to manage multiple vehicles and ensure that they are being used efficiently.

Title: Add Expense
URL: https://helpdesk.uffizio.com/knowledge/expenses

Add Expense
Expenses are the costs incurred in managing and maintaining assets or objects in the fleet. These include a wide range of costs such as fuel, maintenance, insurance, taxes, and more.
Expenses are categorised into two types:
Variable
or
Fixed.
Variable expenses
are costs that arise unpredictably or suddenly and do not follow a fixed schedule. The expenses related to accidents, fuel, fines, tolls, and other unforeseen events can be categorised as variable expenses.
Fixed expenses
are predictable costs that occur at regular, scheduled intervals. The expenses include insurance premiums, taxes, and driver salaries, which are incurred consistently over time.
The software allows users to add expenses individually or in bulk. It also offers detailed reports and charts, enabling effective data analysis and informed decision-making for fleet management.
Please Note:
The Expense module is available exclusively in the Standard and Premium versions of the platform.
To Get Started
Log in to your account.
Go to
Settings > Master > Expense.
Upon clicking on Expense, users will be taken to the Expenses overview page, where they can manage and review all their expense details.

Title: Overview of Job
URL: https://helpdesk.uffizio.com/knowledge/job-module

Overview of Job
The
Job Module in the platform is designed to streamline task assignment and management processes for fleet operations. This feature enables efficient tracking, monitoring, and completion of tasks assigned to drivers, vehicles, or other operational staff to improve their overall efficiency.
Key Features of Job Module:
Job Creation and Task Assignment:
Assign jobs to drivers or vehicles with clear deadlines and priorities.
Incorporate checkpoints with estimated visit times and halt durations for detailed monitoring.
Convenience to create jobs from previously created jobs or use playback options for faster creation.
Add instructions, checklists, or documents for better task clarity.
Job Scheduling:
Plan and organize jobs based on specific needs and preferences.
By allowing customization of job parameters, such as convoy objects, object load status, estimated completion times, and specific routes, fleet managers can ensure that each job is tailored to achieve maximum efficiency.
Optimize workflow for improved productivity and resource utilization.
Real-Time Tracking:
Track job progress and status in real time from the web platform and driver application.
Compare estimated and actual completion times and distances to evaluate performance.
Notification System:
Receive automatic alerts for status changes, significant updates, and task deadlines to stay informed and ensure timely action.
Performance Analytics:
Generate reports on task completion rates, delays, and driver performance.
Identify operational bottlenecks and optimize processes.
Learn more about
Adding a job
Downloading job details
Access Job through Driver Application
Please Note:
The Job module is exclusively available with the
Premium
version of the platform.

Title: Add Job
URL: https://helpdesk.uffizio.com/knowledge/add-job

Add Job
Users have the ability to enhance their work assignment processes, optimize route planning, and manage tasks effectively, thereby improving the efficiency and convenience of job scheduling.
They can create jobs either individually or in bulk. This document serves as a comprehensive guide on how to create a job.
To Create a Job
Log in to your account.
Go to
Settings > Master > Job.
Upon clicking on Job, you will be taken to the jobs overview page, where you can view all existing job records.
Watch :
How to configure Job.
Click
on the
➕
button on the taskbar.
The
Job Planning
screen will now be displayed.
Select the appropriate
Company
and
Branch
from the drop-down menu under which you wish to create the job.
Provide the
Name
and
Description
of the job to ensure clear identification and understanding of the task.
Choose the
Job Type
that best fits your requirement.
Without Object:
This feature enables job creation with a defined route and specific conditions without allocating an object, allowing the same job to be utilized later for multiple objects. This enhances efficiency by eliminating the need to recreate identical jobs.
With Object:
Choose the "With Object" option if you wish to create a job that involves a specific object.
Assign To:
Choose the vehicle from the drop-down list that you wish to assign for this job.
Select
Representative
from the dropdown list if a representative is involved with the job.
To assign a
Representative
for the job, it is essential to first create a representative from the driver screen, ensuring their role is designated as "Representative." Please note that only representatives associated with the selected company will appear in the drop-down list for your selection.
Consider Via:
Select the appropriate option to determine how the checkpoint is considered visited based on the condition set.
Map:
Choose this option to mark a checkpoint as visited when the vehicle reaches its location on the map.
QR Code:
Select this option to mark a checkpoint as visited by scanning the QR code.
Once this option is selected, you will get the QR code download option beside the checkpoint. Also, you can download the QR code for all the
Convoy:
A convoy is a group of vehicles traveling together on the same route for safety, efficiency, or coordination, ensuring timely delivery, shared resources, and enhanced security during transit.
To enable the Convey option, please check the corresponding box.
Objects:
Select the desired objects that you want to add as a convoy from the dropdown list.
Convoy Tolerance:
This refers to the allowed distance between vehicles in a convoy for effective coordination during transit, with a default setting of 200 meters that can be adjusted as needed.
Object Load State:
Choose the current status of the load on the vehicle during the job from the dropdown menu, or feel free to add a new status if necessary.
Upload File:
You have the option to upload any relevant documents related to the job for easy access and reference.
Schedule Type:
Schedule the job according to your specific needs.
Relative:
Select Relative if you want to create a schedule that repeats on a timely basis.
Select the
Schedule
as per requirement.
Daily:
Select Daily if you wish to schedule the job to occur on a daily basis.
Weekly:
Choose this option to schedule a job that recurs every week. You can then specify the particular days of the week on which you would like the job to occur.
Monthly:
Choose this option if you wish to schedule a job that occurs once a month. You will then select the specific dates for the job's monthly schedule.
Please input the
Estimated Start Time, Estimated End Time,
and the
Force Close Duration
in the respective fields.
Please choose the start and end dates in the
Valid From
and
Valid To
fields using the date picker to define the validity period for the job.
Fixed:
To create a Fixed schedule that occurs at a specific time without repetition, please select the Fixed option.
Force Close Duration:
Specify the duration after which incomplete jobs should auto-closed.
Start-End Time:
Select specify the start and end date and time for the job.
Automatic:
Choose the Automatic option to establish a schedule that operates independently of time constraints.
Please choose the start and end dates in the
Valid From
and
Valid To
fields using the date picker to define the validity period for the job.
Extra Field:
You can include additional job details such as
Invoice Number, Shipment Number, Product, Quantity,
and
Consignee Name.
To Create Job Route
Copy From:
You can copy the job configuration from any existing created job or from the playback of the object.
Previous Job
: Choose this option to copy details from a previous job. Select the desired job from the dropdown list.
Playback
: Use this option to copy route details from a past playback of the vehicle. Select the desired playback entry from the dropdown list.
Add Start and End Points:
Select this option to include the start and end points in the job.
Checkpoints with reach time:
Choose this option if you require the vehicle to visit checkpoints at specific times.
Consider Job with Route:
Use this option to associate the job with a specific route only.
Route Tolerance (meters)
: Specify the allowable deviation from the route. An alert will be triggered if the vehicle exceeds this tolerance. The default route tolerance is 50 meters but can be adjusted as needed.
Job Start Buffer Time (minutes):
Define the additional time allowed before the scheduled job start time. This buffer ensures flexibility in accommodating delays.
Please Note: Checkpoints with reach time
and
Job Start Buffer Time (minutes)
will not be considered during the automatic job.
To Add Checkpoints
Click on the
➕
button.
Search Location:
Choose the desired option from either the Map or Address Book to locate the checkpoint.
Search the location of the checkpoint in the search bar.
Enter the
Name
of the checkpoint.
Checkpoint State:
You can specify the type of the checkpoint, such as loading or unloading, and add a new checkpoint state if needed.
Form:
You can create a custom form for the checkpoint, such as the loading or unloading point, to capture necessary verification details before the vehicle is allowed entry, ensuring efficient data collection during the job process.
The form that you create within the designated company and branch will be available for selection in the list.
Location:
The address of the checkpoint will be displayed in this field.
Select the
Radius
of the checkpoint.
Add as Address:
Select this option if you want to add the location as an address.
Click on
Save
to add the checkpoint.
To Add Checkpoints in Bulk
Click on the Upload button.
Download the sample file
using the provided link, complete the necessary information in the specified format, and then upload the completed file.
Check the box if you want to
Add
the checkpoint locations
as Address
.
Click on
Save
to add the checkpoints.
Click on the
Save 💾
icon to save the entire job
.
Elock Authentication and Alert Creation with Job
The platform offers Elock authentication to prevent unauthorized activity with ELock while the vehicle is on the job. This feature ensures that the Elock remains secure, requiring an OTP for unlocking at any time during the job.
Furthermore, users can assign specific rights to enable the Elock at particular checkpoints, enhancing security and control over its operation.
When setting up a job for Elock devices, users have the option to configure alerts conveniently from the job creation screen.
Please Note:
The
SMS Configuration
or
Email Configuration
is required to get the OTP for Elock Authentication
.
To Create Job from Live Tracking Screen
Users can conveniently create a job directly from a tooltip widget located on the live tracking screen, enhancing the efficiency of the job assignment process.
To create a job, simply click on the
➕ Job
button, and a job configuration window will appear. You can then proceed to follow the job creation steps outlined earlier in this document.
To Create Job from Playback
To add a job for the current playback, the user has the ability to do it directly from the Playback screen on Live Tracking. This feature allows for real-time job assignment based on the ongoing route of the vehicle, enhancing operational efficiency.
To initiate the job creation process, simply click on the Create Job icon, as indicated in the image above. This action will open the job configuration screen, utilizing the current playback as the designated route for the job.
To Add Expense for Job
The system allows you to incorporate expenses associated with the job, enabling comprehensive tracking and management of costs. For detailed instructions, refer to the
Adding Expenses
section.

if you have checked the box
it means that the form can be used to assign to checkpoints.
if you have unchecked the box
it means that the form can't be used to assign to checkpoints.

write the name of the field.

select the type of field you are adding from the list.

eg: if you have written the Label as Door and selected the type as checkbox in values you can write Door handle, Door screw, Door Lock etc.
eg: if you have written the Label as gender and selected the type as Radio in values you can write Male,Female.
In
Default Values
you can write the default values that will be used before the driver changes it.
eg: if you have written the Label as Condition and selected the Textarea you can set the default value as Good.
In
Validation
select the condition you want to set for the Label.
eg: if you have selected the Type as textarea you can set the validaton as alphabet. so in that label only alphabet can be written and nothing else.
In the
Place holder
you can write a text of what the person needs to write in the box.
eg: if you have written the Label as gender and selected the type as Textarea in placeholder you can write ," please write gender " .which will be displayed in the field.

You can enter what should be the maximum length of the property.
In
Min limit
you can enter the min limit of characters that needs to be entered in the field.

Title: Route Optimization Feature
URL: https://helpdesk.uffizio.com/knowledge/route-optimization

Route Optimization Feature
Route optimization is the process of determining the most efficient route for a vehicle or object and ensuring that selected vehicles are utilized effectively for assigned jobs. This feature helps save time, reduce fuel consumption, improve operational efficiency, lower transportation costs, and boost productivity. Jobs are automatically created using route optimization, streamlining job assignments, and ensuring optimal resource utilization.
Please Note:
The Route Optimization feature is exclusively available in the
Premium
version of the platform.
Watch :
How to use route optimisation.
To Optimize the Route
Log in to your account.
Go to
Settings > Master > Route Optimization
Select the
Optimization Based On
option from the drop-down list to choose the criteria for route optimization.
Distance:
Select the Distance option if your goal is to optimize the route primarily based on distance.
Select the
Company
from the dropdown list to define which company's vehicles or assets will be included in the route optimization process.
Select the
Objects
from the dropdown list to specify the vehicles or assets that need to be included for route planning.
Enter the
Radius
of the points to set the distance within which the optimization should occur, ensuring that the routes stay within the specified radius.
Distance with weight:
Select Distance with Weight if you want to optimize the route based on the distance along with the weight of the load.
Select the
Company
from the dropdown list to define which company's vehicles or assets will be included in the route optimization process.
Select the
Load Type:
Full or Partial.
Choose the appropriate
Product Type
that corresponds to the load on the vehicle from the drop-down list.
Select the
Unit
of the product or load on the vehicle from the drop-down list.
Select the
Objects
from the dropdown list to specify the vehicles or assets that need to be included for route planning.
Enter the
Radius
of the points to set the distance within which the optimization should occur, ensuring that the routes stay within the specified radius.
To add a start point, click on the
➕
button.
Search Location
in the search bar. Utilize the marker to pinpoint the exact location.
Click on the
Save 💾 icon.
To add delivery point:
Click on the
➕
button for uploading delivery points one by one.
Search Location
in the search bar. Utilize the marker to pinpoint the exact location.
Click on the
Save 💾 icon.
Click on the upload button for bulk uploading delivery points.
Download the sample file
from the link given. The file will hold the basic information about the delivery points.
After you have entered all the necessary information, please upload the XLS file using
Choose File
option.
Click on the
Save 💾 icon.
Click on
Optimize Route
.
To create a job of all trips:
Click on the
➕
button.
Select the
Start-End Time
of the job from the date and time picker.

.

of the trip.

of the job from the date and time picker.

(optional).

Title: Eco Driving/Driver Rating
URL: https://helpdesk.uffizio.com/knowledge/eco-driving

Eco Driving/Driver Rating
The Eco Driving or Driver Rating feature within the software empowers users to effectively monitor and assess driver performance. It is based on various factors such as harsh braking, fuel efficiency, and obedience to safety regulations and rules.
Driver rating uses the object's data to provide a complete view of the driver's performance. The user can set penalty points for the drivers based on their driving habits, considering parameters like harsh braking, harsh acceleration, speeding, idling, ADAS, and DMS violations. The system will assign scores to the drivers based on these points and provide the user with the driver rating.
Please Note:
The Eco Driving/Driver Rating is included only in the Standard and Premium versions of the platform.
To Get Started
Log in to your account.
Go to
Settings > Master > Eco Driving / Driver Rating.
After clicking on Eco Driving, you will be directed to the Driver Rating Overview screen, where you can have a look at all your Driver Rating records.

Title: Add Object Group
URL: https://helpdesk.uffizio.com/knowledge/object-group

Add Object Group
Object Group is a collection of related objects that are clubbed together to form a group in order to manage collectively. An object group allows the users to organize their objects into groups based on their type, location, or any other criteria that they would like to define as per their preferences and requirements.
For example, users can create an object group of all the objects at a particular worksite; or they can create an object group that consists of all the objects; or they can create an object group that has all the vehicles of the same type.
Object groups help users efficiently manage and monitor their assets by offering a unified perspective of their current status. Object groups can be utilized on the live tracking screen to efficiently filter objects, facilitate the creation of company subusers, and set up alerts.
Please Note:
Object Group is included only in
Standard
and
Premium
variations of the platform.
To Get Started
Log in to your account.
Go to
Settings > Master > Object Group.
Upon clicking on
Object Group
, users will be directed to the Object Group Overview screen, where they can view and manage all existing Objects groups.

Company
from the drop-down list under which you want to create an object group.

for the object group to facilitate easy reference and identification.

of the object group.
Choose the

you wish to include in the object group.

Title: Classify Trips
URL: https://helpdesk.uffizio.com/knowledge/classify-trip

Classify Trips
Classify Trips refers to the process of classifying a trip based on its intended purpose or type.
A trip can be classified into three types: Business Trip, Personal Trip, and Inactive trip, based on its intent.
In the system, a trip is defined as the duration from when the ignition is turned ON until it is turned OFF for the vehicle.
Please Note:
Classify Trips is included only in
Premium
version of the platform.
Watch :
How to classify trips.
To Get Started
Log in to your account.
Go to
Settings > Master > Classify Trips.
Select
Company
and
Branch
from the dropdown list.
Choose the
Date
for which you wish to classify the trips using the date picker.
Select the
Object
of which the trips are to be classified.
Click on the
Apply
button.
The page you will navigate to presents the trip details for the selected vehicle within the specified time range.
Click on the
Edit
⁣
icon
to classify the trip.
Choose the appropriate
Trip Status
from the drop-down menu, selecting from the categories: business trip, personal trip, or invalid trip.
Select the
Vendor
of the trips from the
drop-down menu.
Enter a
Note
to add additional information about the trip if required.
Click on the
Save
💾
button.
Classified trips can be accessed in the reports, where they are organized based on their distance and duration for easier analysis.

Title: Send Command
URL: https://helpdesk.uffizio.com/knowledge/send-command

Send Command
The Send Command feature enables users to remotely send specific commands to the GPS devices installed in vehicles. This functionality allows for the execution of various actions or configurations on the device via GPRS.
There are two ways to send commands to the device:
SMS Commands
(
SMS Service Configuration
is required) and
GPRS commands
.
The users have the ability to send these commands from two different screens on the platform: the
Send command
screen and the
Live tracking
screen.
Watch :
How to Configure Send Command.
To Get Started
Log in to your account.
Go to
Settings > Master > Send Command.
Upon navigating to the
Send Command
screen, you will be directed to the
Send Command Overview
page, where you can view a history of all previously sent commands.
To Send Command to Multiple Vehicles At the same time
Click
on the
➕
button on the taskbar.
Select the
Company
from the dropdown list.
Select the
Device Type
from the dropdown list.
Based on the device type selected, the objects under the selected company will be displayed. Select the
Object
from the dropdown list to which you would like to send the command.
Select the
Type
of command to be sent.
SMS:
SMS commands are often used in situations where a direct internet connection or data service is not available or practical.
Please Note:
When an SMS command is sent, a response from the device will not be received.
GPRS:
GPRS commands are typically used to communicate with devices or sensors that are equipped with GPRS connectivity.
Please Note:
When a GPRS command is sent, the user can expect to receive a response from the device.
Select the
Command
from the list that you would like to send.
If you have selected a Custom command, enter the
Message
that you would like to send as a command.
Choose the appropriate
Schedule For
option based on your requirements.
Now:
When you select Now, the command will be sent at the current time.
One Time:
When you select One Time, the command will be sent only once at the
Execution Time
selected.
Hourly:
When you select Hourly, the command will be sent every hour at the minute selected in
Executed Hour
.
Daily:
When you select Daily, the command will be sent daily at the time selected in
Execution Time
.
Weekly:
When you select Weekly, the command will be scheduled to send weekly on the days selected in
Execution Day
and time selected in
Execution
Time
.
Monthly:
When you select Monthly, the command will be scheduled to send every month on the date selected in
Execution Day
and time selected in
Execution Time.
The system will attempt to send the command multiple times within the
Validity
period you specify, continuing until a response is received from the device. If the device does not respond, the command will be marked as inactive, and the reason for failure will be displayed in the
History
popup.
Click on the
Save 💾
icon
to send the command at the scheduled time.
To Send Command from the Live Tracking Screen
Log in to your account.
Go to
Live Tracking.
On the
Object tab
, you will find the
</>
icon against each vehicle, which is the Send Command button.
To Send Command to a Single Object
Click on the
</>
icon on the Object tab.
Select the
Type
of command to be sent.
Select the
Command
from the list that you would like to send.
Enter the
Message
that you would like to send as a command.
Select the
Schedule For
based on your requirements.
The system will try sending the command for the time period you select in
Validity
until the device responds.
Click on the
Send
button to send the command at the scheduled time.
To Download Command Details
Log in to your account.
Go to
Settings > Master > Send Command.
Click on the Download button on the taskbar.
A file with an
XLS
extension gets downloaded.
You may distribute this file to others or utilize it for your specific purposes as needed.
To send commands from the mobile application, click
here
.
To download the command details from the mobile application, click
here
.

Add Announcement
An announcement is a formal notification or message intended to inform users about important updates, changes, or events. In the context of the platform, it typically includes information such as new features, system updates, maintenance schedules, or other relevant news.
Announcements are typically visible to all users and can be delivered through notifications, or via email or SMS, based on the preferences selected during the announcement process. These messages may appear in the notifications section or as pop-ups when logged into the application.

Title: Base Location Configuration
URL: https://helpdesk.uffizio.com/knowledge/base-location-configuration

Base Location Configuration
Base Location Configuration is a feature on our platform that allows users to define a central or primary location for their operations, such as a depot, warehouse, or headquarters. This location serves as a reference point for various functionalities, including:
Monitoring Movement:
Track vehicle departures and arrivals relative to the base location.
Performance Metrics:
Measure critical metrics such as the distance traveled from the base and time spent at the base location.
Geofence Integration:
Set up geofences around the base location to streamline trip creation and monitoring while activating alerts or notifications for specific events.
This feature helps streamline operations, enhance monitoring, and improve overall fleet management.
Please Note:
Base Location Configuration is available only with the Premium version of the platform.
Before You Get Started
Create the geofence for each base location to enable efficient trip creation utilizing those designated geofences. Learn how to create
Geofence
.
To Get Started
Log in to your account.
Go to
Settings > Master > Base Location Configuration.
Upon clicking on
Base Location Configuration,
you will be directed to the
Base Location Configuration Overview
page, where you can have a look at all the records.
Click on the ➕ button on the taskbar.
Select the
Company
and
Branch
from the drop-down list.
Consider:
Select the appropriate option from the categories of Object, Object Type, or Object Group to add the desired object to the object list.
According to your selection, the relevant objects will be displayed in the drop-down list. Please choose the appropriate
Object
for the base location configuration.
Select if
Trip start and end geofence are the same
.
No:
Select No if the trip start and end geofence are not same
Select the
Configuration
for the trip.
One Way:
Select one way if the trip is a one-way journey.
Choose the appropriate
Base Location Start
geofence from the drop-down menu.
Choose the appropriate
Base Location End
geofence from the drop-down menu.
Return:
Select return if the trip is intended to be a return journey.
Choose the appropriate
Base Location Start
geofence from the drop-down menu.
Choose the appropriate
Base Location End
geofence from the drop-down menu.
Provide the estimated duration of the trip in hours in
Approx Duration
.
Provide the estimated distance for the trip in kilometers (km) in
Approx Distance
.
Choose the
Trip start/end condition
from the available options that best aligns with your requirements.
Yes:
Select Yes if the trip start and end geofence are same.
Choose the appropriate
Base Location Start
geofence from the dropdown list.
Select the
Trip start/end condition
.
Valid From:
Choose the start date and time to establish the validity period for the configuration.
Valid To:

Click on the

icon.

Title: Add Geofence
URL: https://helpdesk.uffizio.com/knowledge/add-geofence

Add Geofence
Geofences represent virtual boundaries established around designated geographical areas. These areas can include various locations, such as warehouses, delivery zones, customer territories, or restricted regions, among others.
Uses of Geofence Feature:
Geofences can be created to monitor vehicle activity within a specific area or to oversee trips between various locations, such as loading and unloading points.
Additionally, users can be notified when a vehicle enters or exits these designated locations.
Geofences are created by specifying GPS coordinates and defining a radius around them. They can be categorized as
area
,
road fence,
stay-in
, or
stay-away
zones.
To Get Started
Users can easily add Geofence one at a time or in bulk using different options on the platform:
Geofence Screen
Live Tracking Screen
Tooltip Widget
Playback Screen
Reports
Watch :
How to add geofence.
To Add Geofence from Geofence Screen
Log in to your account.
Go to
Settings > Master > Geofence.

Geofence
, you will be directed to the
Geofence Overview
page, where you can view and manage all the geofence records.
To Create Geofences Individually
Click
on the
➕
button on the taskbar.
Select the
Reseller
and
Company
from the drop-down list.
Provide the
Name
of the geofence.
Select the
Category
of the geofence from the drop-down list.
Select the appropriate
Geofence Access
option to define the visibility and accessibility of geofences for users:
Public:
Choose this option if the geofence should be visible to all users.
Private:
Choose this option to ensure the geofence is visible only to the user who created it.
Select the
Geofence Group
from the drop-down list to categorize the geofence based on its type or specific use case. If no suitable group exists, you can create a new one.
Choose the appropriate
Geofence Type
from the dropdown list, or if the desired type is not available, you have the option to create a new one.
Enter the
Contact No
of the responsible authority of that area.
Provide the specific
Address
of the geofence location.
You can assign different colors to the geofence for easy identification by type or use case. Select the color from the
Color Picker.
Choose the
Tolerance
from the dropdown list, as this setting will assist in defining a radius. This will ensure accurate tracking of geofence entries and exits.
Provide a
Description
if necessary to clarify the purpose or details of the geofence.
On the Map, search and select the desired
Location
.
Draw a geofence in either a
Polygon
,
Rectangle
or
Circle
shape as per your requirement.
Polygonal Geofence:
Rectangular Geofence:
