Title: How to create Duns number
URL: https://helpdesk.uffizio.com/knowledge/how-to-create-duns-number

How to create Duns number
To create a D-U-N-S (Data Universal Numbering System) Number, you'll need to follow a few steps. The D-U-N-S number is a unique nine-digit identifier assigned to a business entity by Dun & Bradstreet (D&B), which is often used for identifying businesses and establishing credibility.
Here’s a step-by-step guide to creating a D-U-N-S number:
Step-by-Step Guide to Get a D-U-N-S Number
Step 1: Check if Your Business Already Has a D-U-N-S Number
Before applying for a new D-U-N-S number, you should first check if your business already has one. You can do this by searching for your business on the Dun & Bradstreet website.
Go to the Dun & Bradstreet website: D&B - D-U-N-S Number Lookup
Search for your business name or address.
If a D-U-N-S number exists for your business, it will show up in the results.
Step 2: Gather Required Information
To apply for a D-U-N-S number, you will need the following information:
Legal Business Name: The name of your company as it appears on legal documents.
Business Address: Physical location of your company.
Phone Number: The main phone number for your business.
Name of the CEO or Business Owner: The individual in charge of the business.
Legal Structure: Whether the business is a corporation, partnership, sole proprietorship, etc.
Year Established: When your business started.
Primary Line of Business: Industry or nature of your business.
Number of Employees: How many people work for your company.
Step 3: Visit the Dun & Bradstreet Website
Navigate to the official Dun & Bradstreet D-U-N-S Number Registration Page:
https://www.dnb.com/duns-number/get-a-duns.html
Step 4: Fill Out the Application Form
On the registration page, click on the "Get a D-U-N-S Number" button.
You will be asked to create an account with Dun & Bradstreet or sign in if you already have one.
Complete the application form with the required details (from Step 2).
Step 5: Submit Your Application
After filling out all the necessary information, review your details carefully to ensure everything is correct.
Submit the application form.
If everything is in order, D&B will process your request.
Step 6: Wait for Processing
The processing time can vary. It may take a few business days to receive your D-U-N-S number if all your details are correct.
Dun & Bradstreet will send you an email once your D-U-N-S number has been assigned.
Step 7: Confirm Your D-U-N-S Number
Once your request is processed, you will receive your D-U-N-S number.
You can verify your D-U-N-S number on the D&B website or through your account dashboard.
Step 8: Use Your D-U-N-S Number
Once you receive your D-U-N-S number, you can use it for business credit, government contracts, partnerships, and other official purposes.
Important Notes:
Free vs. Paid Service: Obtaining a D-U-N-S number is free if you're applying for one for standard business needs. However, D&B also offers premium services, such as monitoring and reporting, that may come at a cost.
Timeframe: In many cases, you can receive your D-U-N-S number within 1-2 weeks, but processing times can vary depending on the volume of requests.
D-U-N-S Number Uses: This number is required by many government agencies, including for grant applications and federal contracts in the U.S., and it can also be useful for establishing business credibility and creditworthiness.

Title: Why all the vehicles on platform are showing inactive ?
URL: https://helpdesk.uffizio.com/knowledge/why-all-the-vehicles-on-platform-are-showing-inactive

Why all the vehicles on platform are showing inactive ?
Vehicle going inactive of the platform can create a panic situation as the user won't be able to track the vehicle. This may lead to a serious consequences if any disaster happens. There could be reason for vehicle going inactive and below are the troubleshooting steps.
Poor internet connection
If the vehicle is in a location with a weak GPRS signal, it might not be able to transmit information to the server to display the data on a live tracking screen.
Check the Internet connection with the help of an SMS command.
For SMS commands, contact the device manufacturer
If there is high network congestion or heavy data traffic in the area, it may slow down the transmission of data from the tracking device.
In such cases, please wait till the network coverage gets better.
GPS device issue
There may be a problem with the specific GPS device if another one of the same model is updating properly on the tracking screen.
You can verify the same by following the above steps for different vehicles.
If the data in the system log is not updating, there may be an issue with the device. You must verify the same from the device end.
Delay in updating the data
The tracking platform may also experience a problem getting the data as a result of which the vehicle's data does not update on the live tracking screen.
To verify
Login to your account.
Click on
Report > Logs > System log
Search for the vehicle number in the
object selection
option
Select
the vehicle and click on
Apply
A system log summary
report would be generated
Double-click on the record to see the detailed view of the system log
Data actual time
refers to the time when the device generates or records the data.
Data received time
refers to the data received on the tracking platform.
History data
refers to records of the device's past locations and movements.
Please Note:
History data are not updated on the live tracking screen.
Please contact support if your data updates match your time zone, there is no past data, and the data status appears green in color.
How to raise ticket on support ?
Malfunctioning tracking device
If all the above settings fail, the problem can be a broken tracking device. If the device isn't working properly, check it out and replace it.
If all the above troubleshooting steps are done and you are still facing the issue, kindly raise a ticket on support.

ticket on support

Title: Why am I getting duplicate IMEI number while adding object ?
URL: https://helpdesk.uffizio.com/knowledge/why-am-i-getting-duplicate-imei-number-while-adding-object

Why am I getting duplicate IMEI number while adding object ?
Each device should have a unique IMEI number to differentiate it from others. If you are encountering duplicate IMEI numbers while adding an object, there could be a few possibility that same device is added on the server.
Data Entry Error
It's possible that there was a data entry error during the process of adding the object. Double-check the IMEI number you are entering to ensure that it is accurate and doesn't contain any typos or mistakes. Even a small error can result in a duplicate IMEI.
To Verify
Login to your
account
Go to
Setting > General > Object
Search for the
IMEI
number which is giving the error.
If same
IMEI
is already added you will be able to see it.
Same device is used with different partner
To cut costs, vendors and end users could both utilise the same equipment. Duplicate IMEI errors may occur if the end user is utilising software that was purchased from a different vendor while using the same server.
Vendor needs to confirm with the end user from where did they purchased the device and also ask the user to delete the IMEI number from old service provider.
Please Note:
We would not be providing details for the vendor with whom the services were running earlier.
System Error
There might be a system error or bug in the software or platform you are using to add the object. In some cases, the system might not properly validate the uniqueness of IMEI numbers, resulting in duplicates. If this is the case, you should reach out to the technical support.
If all the above steps are done and you are still facing the issue, kindly raise a ticket for support.

ticket on support
?

Why I am unable to get the alert notification of ignition on and off?
Alerts are important because they serve as notifications or warnings about specific events or conditions that require attention. Possible reasons for alerts not generating are listed below.
Incorrect alert configuration.
Alerts would only be generated if the configuration is properly done on the system.

Configure the alert from the
Web portal
Configure the alert from the
Mobile application
The ignition alerts will work only if it meets the criteria i.e Ignition turned
ON
or
OFF
.
Ignition port is not configured
To verify,

Double click on the
Object
..
Click on
Sensor
tab.
Enable on
Ignition port
if it is not enabled.
Ignition data needs to be correct

and

Why am I unable to immobilize the vehicle?
Several factors can contribute to challenges encountered during immobilization. Below are some typical issues along with troubleshooting steps to help resolve them
Verify that the user has the appropriate permissions to access the Immobilise feature.
Verify the device's network settings by ensuring it is connected to a stable and reliable network. You can confirm this by checking the system log report to see if the device is updating with the current time.
Make sure that the appropriate immobilizer sensor is properly connected to both the platform and the hardware.
How to Check Connectivity on the Platform
How to check connectivity on Hardware
You can check the connectivity of the hardware by sending SMS commands to immobilize the vehicle. If the SMS commands do not successfully immobilize the vehicle, this may indicate a potential issue with the hardware connection.

Title: Why am I receiving an incorrect alert time?
URL: https://helpdesk.uffizio.com/knowledge/why-am-i-unable-to-see-the-alert-overview

Why am I receiving an incorrect alert time?
Here are a few possibilities and solutions if you're having issues with alert times that don't match the time the event actually occurred as presented.
Timezone settings
In the application where you are viewing the alerts, check the timezone settings. Ensure that your local time is properly configured as the system's timezone.
Check that each user's timezone settings are configured properly if the system contains users from multiple time zones.
To verify
Login to your account.

Title: Why am I unable to receive an SMS alert?
URL: https://helpdesk.uffizio.com/knowledge/unable-to-send-sms

Why am I unable to receive an SMS alert?
There could be several reasons why you are unable to send an SMS alert. Here are a few reasons and troubleshoot the issue:
SMS API stops working
To verify
Login to your
account.
Got to
Setting
> General > Admin/
Reseller
/ Company.
Double-click on the account for which you want to configure SMS.
Click on the
SMS
tab.
Run the API in the browser to confirm if it working. Outputs are different as per the provider.
If any modification required in authentication
i.e. User name
,
Password
or
Sender
ID
etc then update working authentication in API and then verify the same.
Verify the SMS balance in API.
Wrong SMS configuration on the Alert
To verify
Login to your account.
Go to
Setting > General > Alert.
Double-click on the
alert
for which SMS alerts are not received.
Make sure the
SMS
option should be checked marked.
SMS Gateway:
Select the type of gateway from the two available.
Inherit
: If the new user wants to use the SMS service created by the parent user.
Custom
: To create a new SMS service.
SMS Gateway URL:
To configure SMS Gateway. If a user has purchased a bulk SMS service and wants to integrate them, then he has to configure the bulk SMS API received from the service provider.
Check for the daily SMS limit with your service provider
There are providers who keep the limit for sending the SMS on daily basis. check with the provider if they have configured any limit for the SMS.
Ensure that the templates configured on the platform precisely match the templates approved by your service provider.
The platform offers the ability to configure customized templates for SMS messages. It is important to note that in certain countries, regulatory authorities may require prior approval of these templates for bulk SMS distribution. If the template used on the platform does not align with the approved version, the SMS may be sent to the SMS gateway but will not be delivered to the recipient.
For further information, we encourage you to refer the dedicated knowledgebase article on
Alert Notification Templates
.

Why does it show server out-of-reach message in the mobile application?
It is a critical issue when you are not able to access the application and getting out of reach message. This problem may occur when an application is unable to connect to the server.
Poor Internet connection
When a mobile device is connected to a weak or poor internet connection, the application tries to connect to the server but unfortunately cannot.
To Verify
Check the internet speed of the service provider.
You can verify the internet speed by
Speed Test.
Switching the network could also help in rectifying the issue.
There are scenarios where you see all the network bars are full in mobile networks and also on Wifi but the bandwidth which is required to connect an application is low. Talk to your service provider once.
Alternatively, you can log into web portal from the same Internet Service provider and check if you are able to access it.
If yes, then report it to us.
Application working with an old version
Application with older version might be the reason for the disturbance.
Features are upgraded and the old version does not support them. To resolve the same kindly update the application.
Please kill the background-running application if the first two methods don't work to solve this issue.

Title: Why is there a data delay in the mobile application?
URL: https://helpdesk.uffizio.com/knowledge/data-delay-in-the-mobile-application

Why is there a data delay in the mobile application?
Most of the users prefer mobile application to track their vehicles. There could be several reasons
why the data is delayed in the mobile application.
Here are a few possible reasons and solutions.
Poor internet connection
When a mobile device is connected to a weak or poor internet connection, data transmission may experience delays.
To Verify
Check the internet speed for the service provider.
You can verify the internet speed by
Speed Test.
Switch to a different internet connection.
If the vehicle is in a location with weak cellular or GPS signal, it might not be able to transmit information to the live tracking screen.
Check the Internet connection with the help of an SMS command.
For SMS commands, contact the device manufacturer
If there is high network congestion or heavy data traffic in the area, it may slow down the transmission of data from the tracking device.
In such cases, please wait till the network coverage gets better.
Delay in updating the data
The tracking platform may also experience a problem getting the data as a result of which the vehicle's data does not update on the live tracking screen.
To verify
Login to your account.
Click on
Report > Logs > System log
Search for the vehicle number in the
object selection
option.
Select
the vehicle and click on
Apply.
A system log summary
report would be generated.
Double-click on the record to see the detailed view of the system log.
Data actual time
refers to the time when the device generates or records the data.
Data received time
refers to the data received on the tracking platform.
History data
refers to records of the device's past locations and movements.
Please Note:
History data are not updated on the live tracking screen.
Click on the
Status
icon to find the reason behind the issue.
Out-dated application version
You need to update the application with the latest version.
To update your application, go to
Google play store
/
Apple store
and update the application with latest version.

Why is my vehicle not coming live?
There may be several reasons why the vehicle is not displayed live on a tracking platform. Some of the reasons and troubleshooting are mentioned below:
Issue with the internet data connection and plan

, device port, and APN configuration

,

, and
APN

through,

Incorrect IMEI number inserted
The
IMEI
inserted on the portal and on the GPS device must match.
Using an SMS command, you can check the GPS device's IMEI number.
You can also check the IMEI number, which is printed on the back of the device.
Problem with the GPS connection
Verify the GPS signal's strength and ensure nothing is obstructing it.
With the use of an SMS command, you can determine the GPS connection.
GPS connection can also be checked through the system log report in your
account
.
To verify
Navigate to
Report > Logs > System log
Click on the
Status
icon to find the reason behind the issue.
Status Icon would be coloured
Red
Check if your SIM card whitelisted or not?

Bangladesh
,
Bhutan
,
India
,
Maldives
,
Nepal
,
Pakistan
, and
Sri Lanka
, with
Afghanistan
frequently included.
Malfunctioning tracking device

Title: Definitions of IP address, Device port, APN
URL: https://helpdesk.uffizio.com/knowledge/ip-address

Definitions of IP address, Device port, APN
IP address
Each device connected to a computer network that makes use of the Internet Protocol is given an
IP address
, also known as an
Internet Protocol address
. It functions as an identifier that makes it possible for devices to find and connect with one another via a network.
IP address will look like the above given image. The number may vary.
Device port
An interface for physical or virtual communication that enables a device to connect to or communicate with other devices or networks is known as a device port. A device port is a specified endpoint for delivering or receiving data through a particular communication protocol in the context of networking and computer systems.
APN
Access Point Name is referred to as APN. It is a unique network configuration parameter that controls how mobile devices connect to the internet or to a mobile network operator's (MNO) data network when discussing mobile telecommunications and mobile devices.

Title: Why is my vehicle's data not updating on the live tracking screen?
URL: https://helpdesk.uffizio.com/knowledge/why-device-is-not-updating-the-time-at-the-live-tracking-screen

Why is my vehicle's data not updating on the live tracking screen?
A vehicle that doesn't update in real-time on the tracking platform may be experiencing a serious problem that needs to be fixed.
Below is a list of possible reasons for a vehicle not updating and their troubleshooting steps:
Poor internet connection
If the vehicle is in a location with weak cellular or GPS signal, it might not be able to transmit information to the live tracking screen.
Check the Internet connection with the help of an SMS command.
For SMS commands, contact the device manufacturer
If there is high network congestion or heavy data traffic in the area, it may slow down the transmission of data from the tracking device.
In such cases, please wait till the network coverage gets better.
Delay in updating the data
The tracking platform may also experience a problem getting the data as a result of which the vehicle's data does not update on the live tracking screen.
To verify
Login to your account.
Click on
Report > Logs > System log
Search for the vehicle number in the
object selection
option
Select
the vehicle and click on
Apply
A system log summary
report would be generated
Double-click on the record to see the detailed view of the system log
Data actual time
refers to the time when the device generates or records the data.
Data received time
refers to the data received on the tracking platform.
History data
refers to records of the device's past locations and movements.
Please Note:
History data are not updated on the live tracking screen.
Click on the
Status
icon to find the reason behind the issue.
Please email
support@uffizio.com
if your data updates match your time zone, there is no past data, and data status appears green in colour.
Please Note -
If GPS device data is updating in the system log and not on the live tracking screen then please contact
support@uffizio.com
GPS device issue
There may be a problem with the specific GPS device if another one of the same model is updating properly on the tracking screen.
You can verify the same by following the above steps for different vehicles.
If the data in the system log is not updating, there may be an issue with the device. You must verify the same from the device end.
Malfunctioning tracking device
If all the above settings fail, the problem can be a broken tracking device. If the device isn't working properly, check it out and replace it.
If all the above troubleshooting steps are done and you are still facing the issue, kindly raise a ticket on support.
How to raise a
ticket on support
?

Title: How to Calculate fuel consumption based on distance and duration ?
URL: https://helpdesk.uffizio.com/knowledge/how-to-calculate-fuel-consumption

How to Calculate fuel consumption based on distance and duration ?
Fuel consumption often known as fuel economy or fuel efficiency, is a measurement of how effectively a vehicle consumes fuel.
Fuel economy measures a vehicle's performance by how far it can go on a given amount of fuel.
To get started
Login to your account
.
Go to
Setting > General > Object.
Double-click on the record for which you want to calculate fuel consumption.
Navigate to
Profile.
To calculate distance based fuel consumption
In the distance based fuel consumption field add km and liter according to your use.
For example- If your vehicle runs 5 km in 1 liter, then you have to configure it accordingly.
Based on that, you will see the total in the
Fuel consumption report
.
To calculate duration based fuel consumption
In the duration based fuel consumption field add hours and liter according to your use.
For example- If your vehicle consumes 5 liter of fuel in 2 hours of running or idling, then based on that, you need to configure it here.
Based on that, you will see the total in the
Fuel consumption report
.
To check fuel consumption report
Navigate to
Report > Fuel > Fuel Consumption.
If you are still facing the issue, kindly raise a ticket for support.

Title: What are the limitations and available options regarding Data Storage?

What are the limitations and available options regarding Data Storage?
As a standard practice, GPS travel data is stored for a period of 90 days. If you require storage beyond this duration, please reach out to our sales team or the Customer Success team for assistance.
The duration for data storage can be adjusted within the limits set for the parent user, ensuring that it does not exceed the maximum allowable period established for the parent account.
To adjust the limit, please navigate to
Settings> General > Reseller/Company > My Account > Data Storage

Title: How to Sell the Devices from Inventory?
URL: https://helpdesk.uffizio.com/knowledge/how-to-sell-the-devices-from-inventory

How to Sell the Devices from Inventory?
Once the devices are added to the Admin account, they can be sold to the Reseller. The Reseller will then sell these devices to the Reseller Subuser, who will ultimately distribute them to the company users.
This document provides a comprehensive guide on the procedures for selling devices to both resellers and reseller subusers, as well as the registration process required for utilizing these devices to add objects.
Before Getting Started
Learn
How to Add Devices to Your Inventory.
To Get Started
Log in to the admin account.
Go to
Settings > Master > Inventory
.
Upon clicking on
Inventory
, you will be directed to the
Inventory Overview
page, where you can have a look at all your device records.
To Sell the Device to Reseller
When an admin wants to sell the devices to the Reseller, the following steps need to be followed:.
Select the Admin user in the left panel to display the available device stock in the right panel.
Please choose the devices you wish to sell to the reseller.
Click on the
Sell
button on the taskbar.
A new window will appear, allowing you to select the
Reseller
to whom you wish to sell the devices.
Once you have made your selection, click on the
Sell
button to complete the transaction, officially transferring the devices to the chosen reseller.
When you click on the admin account name, you will be able to view the reseller name, the available quantity of devices, and the total number of devices associated with the users.
In the right-side window, you will find the device details, including a comprehensive history of each device’s purchase and sale records.
To sell the devices to the Reseller Subuser
When you click on the admin account name in left-side panel and then select the reseller, you will be able to view the reseller subuser to whom the devices need to be sold.
To sell the devices to the
Reseller subuser;
Choose the
Reseller
from the list provided.
Navigate to the right-side panel to select the devices from the available stock list and choose the devices you wish to sell.
Once the devices to be sold are selected, click on the
Sell
button.
Upon successful completion of the device sale, the number of available devices will be clearly indicated next to the Reseller Subuser's account on the left side of the screen for your easy reference.
To Return the Devices to the Admin/ Reseller
In the event that a device is found to be faulty or for any other reason, the Reseller or Reseller Subuser has the option to return the device back to its parent.
Click on the user whose device needs to be returned back to the superior user in the hierarchy, and you would be able to see the device details on the right side window.
To initiate the return process, please select the device you wish to return from the list displayed in the right-side panel.
After selecting the devices, click on the
Return
button.
In the popup box, select the relevant
Reason Type
and provide additional details if necessary, then click on Return.
Upon clicking the
Return
button, the devices will be reassigned to either the Reseller or Admin based on the established hierarchy. You will find these devices listed in the left-side panel under the appropriate user.
If an incorrect device entry occurs, you can easily remove the devices by utilizing the
Delete
Button located on the taskbar.
To Utilize this Device for Adding Objects
Once the device has been sold to the Reseller Subuser, they can effectively utilize the device to add the object and create a company account via the mobile application by entering the IMEI number.
To Download the QR Code
To utilize this device for object registration, you can use the
downloadable QR code
.
Select the admin account name and click on the reseller name to view detailed information about the reseller subuser, including the total number of devices allocated to them.
When you click the download button, the QR code will be saved to your device. The Reseller Subuser will provide this QR code to the user to sign up for the mobile application.
To do so, you will need to download the
mobile application
from the Play Store or App Store.
Sign Up in Mobile Application
Click on
Sign Up
button on the Sign In page.
Enter the
IMEI
by either manually inputting it or by scanning the QR code that has been provided by the reseller subuser.
You will need to provide the following details for
Registration
.
Plate Number:
Provide the unique plate number of the object being registered.
Company Name:
Specify the company name associated with the account.
Set Up Login Credentials:
Enter a
Username
and
Password
for the account.
Re-type the password to confirm it and ensure accuracy.
Project:
The project associated with the account will be displayed here. This refers to the specific project under which the reseller subuser operates and where the IMEI is registered.
Mobile Number:
Provide the mobile number of the user for whom the account is being created.
After clicking on the
Register
button, the system will create the user account, and the object will be successfully added to the platform.
To Add the Object from Web Platform
Go to
Settings > General > Object
.
Select the Reseller and Reseller Subuser from the drop-down list.
In the IMEI number field, a list of all available IMEI numbers will be displayed as you search for the specific IMEI.
When you select the desired IMEI number, the system will automatically fill in the Device Type based on the device information stored in your inventory.
Fill in the rest of the details required to add the object.
Click on
the
Save 💾
button to create an object.

Trakzee Driver Application
provides a quick dashboard view showing the driver’s status, check-in time, assigned vehicle, and key modules such as Tire Management, Expenses, Classified Trips, Inspection, Completed Jobs, and Pending Jobs. Each card displays basic summaries, and tapping on any section redirects the driver to its detailed module for further actions.

Title: Add Beacon
URL: https://helpdesk.uffizio.com/knowledge/beacon

Add Beacon
A beacon is a small wireless device that uses Bluetooth or similar technologies to transmit signals detected by nearby devices. It helps determine location, track assets, or trigger actions such as sending notifications, commonly used in retail, logistics, and transportation to improve operations and user experiences.
The system enables you to register beacons on the platform, allowing them to connect automatically with any devices that come within their range. Once connected, the system displays the beacon's association with the device, enabling seamless tracking and monitoring of the beacon's location.
Users can easily add beacons to the system, either individually or in bulk.
Watch :
How to Add beacons.
To Get Started
Login to your account.
Go to
Settings > General > Beacon.
Upon clicking on the
Beacon
, you will be directed to the
Beacon Overview
page, where you can easily view and manage all beacon records.
To Add Beacons Individually
Click on the ➕ button on the taskbar.
Reseller
: Choose the appropriate reseller from the dropdown list.
Company
: Pick the corresponding company from the dropdown list.
Branch
: Select the relevant branch from the dropdown list.
UUID
: Input the UUID of the beacon.
Beacon Name
: Provide an informative name for the beacon to facilitate easy identification.
To Upload Beacons in Bulk
Click on the Upload button on the taskbar.
Reseller
: Choose the appropriate reseller from the dropdown list.
Company
: Pick the corresponding company from the dropdown list.
Branch
: Select the relevant branch from the dropdown list.
Download the sample file
from the link given. The file will hold the basic information about the beacon.
Upload
the XLS file after filling up the details.
Click on the
Save 💾 icon.

Title: Access Connected Beacon Data
URL: https://helpdesk.uffizio.com/knowledge/access-connected-beacon-data

Access Connected Beacon Data
Users can easily monitor the beacons connected to tracking devices using the live tracking screen's tooltip widget and beacon tab. This functionality provides real-time insight into the associations between beacons and devices.
Additionally, users have the option to access detailed beacon logs in the reports section, where they can review historical data and track beacon activities for further analysis.
Before Getting Started
Check how to
Add Beacon
on the platform.
To Access Conneccted Beacon Data
Login to your account.
Go to
Live Tracking.
There are two ways to check the connected beacon data:
Beacon Tab
: This section offers an in-depth overview of the beacons, detailing their connection status—whether connected or disconnected—as well as providing relevant information and associated data.
For detailed instructions on viewing the data in the Beacon Tab,
click here.
Tooltip Widget
: The tooltip widget available on the live tracking screen displays real-time information about the beacons connected to tracking devices.
To access the connected beacon information, please follow these steps:
Click on the specific object from the
Object List.
Navigate to
Tooltip
which appears on the right side of the screen.
You will find the
Beacon
widget. Ensure that the beacon widget is activated in the tooltip settings. If it is currently disabled, please enable it to access the necessary information.
When you
click on the connected count
displayed in the image above, a popup will appear, providing you with detailed information about the connected beacons.
The information includes essential details such as the vehicle name, beacon name, UUID, distance between the beacon and the device, beacon frequency, as well as other relevant beacon-related data as illustrated in the below image.

Title: Schedule Trip Classification
URL: https://helpdesk.uffizio.com/knowledge/schedule-trip-classification

Schedule Trip Classification
Schedule Trip Classification refers to the process of classifying a scheduled trip based on its intended purpose or type.
A scheduled trip can be classified into two types: Business Trip, Personal Trip or Unclassified Trip based on its intent.
In the system, a trip is defined as the duration from when the ignition is turned ON until it is turned OFF for the vehicle.
Please Note:
Classify Trips is included only in
Premium
version of the platform.
Watch :
How to configure Schedule Trip Classification.
To Get Started
Log in to your account.
Go to
Settings > Master > Schedule Trip Classification.
you will find the list of previously created scheduled trip classification.
To  create a new schedule click on the ➕ button on the taskbar.
Select
Reseller
from the drop-down.
Select
Company
from the drop-down.
In the
Schedule
field, enter the name you want to assign to this schedule.
In the
Trip Classification
This is a dropdown menu used while scheduling a trip, where you can select the trip type either Personal, Business or Unclassifed.
In the
Schedule Time From
field, set the time from which the system will automatically classify the trip.
In the
Weekdays
field, select the days on which the trip classification should apply.
Click on the
Save 💾
icon
to save the schedule trip classification.
Please Note:
you can see the classified trips in the Trip Classification report.

Title: Manage DVIR
URL: https://helpdesk.uffizio.com/knowledge/manage-dvir

Manage DVIR
Users can perform DVIR inspections regularly to check the health and safety of their vehicles. They can also download the DVIR reports for records or compliance needs.
DVIR is performed by the driver using the Driver's Application from the predefined Templete.
From Manage DVIR  you can create a custom DVIR templete based on Vehicle Type.
To Get Started
Log in to your account.
Go to
Settings > DVIR > Manage DVIR.
To create a new DVIR templete click on the
➕
button on the taskbar.
In the
Inspection Template
, enter a name to easily identify this template.
In
Object Type
, select the object type from the list.
In
Inspection type
, select from Pre trip, Post trip or Both.
Pre trip -  if you want to use this template before a trip starts.
Post trip -  if you want to use this template after trip ends.
Both - if you want to use this template in both the situations
In
Driver signature
, select the signature requirement.
Please note
: In Driver signature, select Mandatory, if you want the driver signature to be Mandatory, select Optional, if you want driver signature to be optional.
To add your addtinal paramaters for inspection click on
Additional Information
button.
In the Label field, enter the custom label for the checkpoint.
Check the mandatory box to make this parameter required.
Click on the bin icon
to delete the checkpoint.
Please note
: In the Label field you can use upto 10 characters.
To select inpection parameters from a predefined list click on the
Add Checkpoint
button
From the
Check point
drop-down select the check point.
From the
sub check point
type
select the points you want to be inspected.
Check the image box if you want to make the image mandatory during inspection.
Check the remark box if you want to make the remark mandatory during inspection.
Click on the bin icon
to delete the checkpoint.
Click on the
Save 💾
icon
to save the custom DVIR.
Please Note
: You must add a main checkpoint ( Add checkpoint ). The DVIR cannot be saved with only an additional checkpoint ( Additional information ).
Watch :
How to configure Manage DVIR.

Title: SOP Definition.

SOP Definition.
An SOP (Standard Operating Procedure) tells what to do when a certain alert is generated.
It helps by giving clear steps or guidance to the user, based on company rules or other needs.
Watch :

To Get Started

Go to
Settings > Master > SOP Definition.
you will find the list of previously created SOP
To  create a new SOP click on the ➕ button on the taskbar.

Reseller
from the drop-down.
Select
Company
from the drop-down.
Select
Branch
from the drop-down.
Select
Alert type
from the drop-down.
Please Note :
In Alert Type you can select alert based on your requirements.

SOP
Box, write your instruction for the specific alert.
Click on the
Save 💾
icon
to save the SOP.

Title: Google Map
URL: https://helpdesk.uffizio.com/knowledge/google-map

Google Map
Overview
Google Maps plays a critical role in Uffizio’s telematics solutions by providing accurate, real-time location data and advanced mapping capabilities. With Google Maps integrated as a third-party service, Uffizio applications—such as Trakzee, SmartBus, and Smart Waste—can visualize vehicles, optimize routes, set geofences, and monitor fleet activities efficiently. This knowledge base explains the purpose, benefits, and implementation of Google Maps within Uffizio services, helping internal teams, clients, and support staff understand how mapping enhances telematics operations.
Introduction to Google Maps
Google Maps
is a widely used mapping platform that provides detailed geographic information, real-time traffic updates, and location-based services. As a
third-party service in Uffizio applications
, Google Maps enables:
Real-Time Vehicle Tracking:
Visualize fleet locations instantly.
Routing & Navigation:
Plan efficient routes considering distance and traffic.
Geofencing:
Create virtual boundaries and receive alerts when vehicles enter or exit specific areas.
Traffic Insights:
Access live traffic data for better route decisions.
Map Visualization:
Display vehicles, trips, stops, and operational points clearly on a map.
In Uffizio, Google Maps serves as the foundation for telematics visualization, while Uffizio adds fleet management, analytics, and operational control capabilities on top of it.
Google Maps Integration Steps
Integrating Google Maps into Uffizio applications involves enabling the required APIs, creating an API key, and configuring billing. The steps below guide internal teams or clients through the process.
Step 1: Create or Log in to Google Cloud Account
Visit
Google Cloud Console
.
Sign in with a Google account.
If you don’t have an account, create one and complete the necessary setup.
Step 2: Create a New Project
Click on the
project dropdown
at the top-left corner.
Click
New Project
.
Enter a
Project Name
(e.g., “Uffizio Telematics”).
Select an
Organization
(if required).
Click
Create
Step 3: Enable Required Google Maps APIs
Go to
APIs & Services > Library
in your project.
Go to Maps under API library
Enable the following APIs based on usage:
Maps JavaScript API
– for embedding interactive maps.
Note
: You can enable the API based on your requirement.
Click
Enable
for each selected API.
Step 4: Set Up Billing
Google Maps Platform requires billing to use APIs.
Go to
Billing > Add Billing Account
.
Enter your payment details.
Link the billing account to your project.
Note: Google provides a free tier monthly credit which can cover small-scale usage.
Step 5: Create an API Key
Navigate to
APIs & Services > Credentials
.
Click
+ Create Credentials → API Key
.
Google will generate a new API key.
Step 6: Restrict the API Key
(Highly Recommended)
Click
Edit API Key
.
Under
Application Restrictions
, choose one:
HTTP referrers
(for web apps)
IP addresses
(for server apps)
Under
API Restrictions
, select the APIs you enabled for this key
Click
Save
.
Step 7:Use Quotas to Limit API Usage
Go to
APIs & Services → Dashboard.
Select your specific API (e.g., Maps JavaScript API).
Click
Quotas
Set
daily or per-minute limits
for requests (e.g., 10,000 requests/day).
Save your configuration.
Note:
When the quota is reached, the API stops serving requests — preventing additional charges.
Step 8: Set Up Budget Alerts
Go to
Google Cloud Console → Billing → Budgets & Alerts.
Click
Create Budget.
Set a
budget amount
(e.g., ₹2,000 or $25).
Configure
alert thresholds
(e.g., 50%, 90%, and 100%).
Google will notify you via email when usage approaches or exceeds your budget.
Note:Use this to stay aware before crossing your preferred monthly spending limit.
Conclusion
Integrating Google Maps into Uffizio’s telematics solutions enhances accuracy, efficiency, and visibility across all applications. From real-time vehicle tracking to route optimization and geofencing, Google Maps acts as the foundation for all location-based services.
To maintain smooth and secure operations, always:
Enable only the APIs you need.
Apply access restrictions for every API key.
Set budgets, quotas, and alerts to control billing.
Monitor usage regularly through the Google Cloud Console.
With the right configuration, Google Maps not only improves functionality but also keeps operational costs predictable and manageable
Helpful Links for Further Reference
🔗
Official Google Resources:
Google Maps Platform Overview
Get API Key for Google Maps Platform
Google Cloud Console
Manage API Usage and Quotas
Set Budgets and Alerts
Best Practices for API Key Security

Title: Machinary Job

Machinary Job
You can create a job for road construction and assign it to the required machinery along with the designated driver. Once the job is created, it will automatically appear in the Trakzee Driver mobile application, allowing the driver to view, manage, and execute the assigned task efficiently.
Please Note:
The Machinary job is available only on Trakzee Premium.
To Get Started
Before you create a machinary job and assign it to driver make sure you have given the machinary job rights to the driver.
Please Note:
You would need to create a sub job that will be assigned to the vehicle. to create a sub job, you would have to create a
Machinary Job
first.

In

select the division from the list. you can click on add new to list a new division, if you have previously created any division it will be listed.

select the Nodal Cluster from the list. you can click on add new to list a new , if you have previously created any Nodal Cluster i

Title: Sub Job
URL: https://helpdesk.uffizio.com/knowledge/sub-job

Sub Job
A subjob is a specific task created under the main machinery job to divide the overall work into smaller, manageable segments. Each subjob can represent an individual activity or portion of the total work subjobs help in tracking progress more precisely, monitoring resource utilization, and ensuring timely completion of each stage of the road construction project.
To Get Started
Log in to your account.
Go to
Settings > Machinary > Sub Job.
Please Note:
Upon clicking the sub job you will be redirected to the overview screen of the subjob.
To Add Sub Job Individually
Click on the
➕
button on the taskbar.
In
Company,
select thivere company from the dropdown under which the sub job is to be performed.
In
Job,
select the Job id under which you want the sub job to be performed.
The
Sub Job ID,
will be assigned automatically by the system.
In
Driver,
select the
driver
to which you want to assign the sub job.
Please Note:
you would need to create a
driver
entity in order to assign a sub job to a driver.
The
State - Operational Region, Zone - Business Division, Sub-Zone - Nodal Cluster, RFP - Work Blocks, Location, Area Supervisor, Territory Supervisor, Nodal Supervisor, Block Supervisor,
will be taken from the main Machinary job that was created.
In
Vehicle,
select the vehicle to which you want to assign the job.
The
Tractor chassis & Machine Chassis,
will be taken from the configuration of the selected vehicle.
Tractor chassis
will be taken from Object/Vehicle chassis no.
Machine Chassis
will be taken from Trailer Name that has been attached to the selected vehicle.
In
Completed Area,
Write the completed area for the sub job.
In
Expected Start Date
, select the date when the job is planned to begin.
In
Expected End Date,
select the date when the job is planned to end.
In
Actual Start Date
, select the date on which the job actually began.
In
Actual End Date
, select the date on which the job actually Ends.
In
Planned Trenching Distance
, enter the total distance (in meters) that is planned to be trenched for the job.
In
Actual Trenching Distance
, enter the total distance (in meters) that has actually been trenched during the job.
In
Marking Done
, select
Yes
if the marking work has been completed, or
No
if it is still pending.
In
Marking Before & Marking After,
you can upload photo for the marking.
In
Status
, select the status from the list. you can click on add new to list a new status, if you have previously created any status it will be listed.
In
Remarks,
You can write the remarks for the sub job.
Click on the
Save 💾 icon
to save the configuration.
To download the created Sub job go on the overview page and click on
icon to download excel format, click on
icon to download in pdf format.

Title: R.A.G Configuration
URL: https://helpdesk.uffizio.com/knowledge/r.a.g-configuration

R.A.G Configuration
The
RAG
feature helps users visually classify driver performance using color indicators —
Red
,
Amber
, and
Green
. These colors represent different performance levels based on the driver’s overall score.
Users can define
custom parameters
as per their company’s requirements. For example, low-performing drivers can be marked in
Red
, average in
Amber
, and good performers in
Green
.
Please Note:
The R.A.G Configuration is included only in the Premium versions of the platform.
To Get Started
Log in to your account.
Go to
Settings > Master > RAG.
After clicking on RAG, you will be directed to the RAG Overview screen, where you can have a look at all your previusly created RAG configuration.
Watch :
How to Configure RAG.
To Create R.A.G
Click on the
➕
button on the taskbar.
The configuration screen of RAG will open
Fom
Company,
select the company for which you want to create the RAG conffiguration.
In
RAG,
write the name of this configuration for indentification.
In
Validity From,
select the from which date this configuration will be used for rating.
In
Distance,
write the minimum distance the vehicle needs to travel after which the RAG configuration will start the rating the vehicle.
In
Harsh Acceleration Score,
Formula can contain only numbers, variables ''a'' and ''t'' and following symbols : +, -, /, *, (, ). you can click on
to see a preview of how the score will function.
Eg;-  a , a+t , a+2, a-2*t.
Variable "a" is Harsh Acceleration Count & Variable "t" is Total Distance.
In
Harsh Braking Score,
Formula can contain only numbers, variables ''b'' and ''t'' and following symbols : +, -, /, *, (, ). you can click on
to see a preview of how the score will function.
Eg:- b , b+t , b+2 , b-2*t.
Variable "b" is Harsh Breaking Count & Variable "t" is Total Distance.
In
Harsh Cornering Score,
Formula can contain only numbers, variables ''c'' and ''t'' and following symbols : +, -, /, *, (, ). you can click on
to see a preview of how the score will function.
Eg:-  c , c+t , c+2 , c-2*t.
Variable "c" is Harsh Cornering Count & Variable "t" is Total Distance.
In
Overspeed Score,
Formula can contain only numbers, variables ''d'' and ''t'' and following symbols : +, -, /, *, (, ).  you can click on
to see a preview of how the score will function.
Eg:-  d , d+t , d+2 , d-2*t.
Variable "d" is Overspeed Duration & Variable "t" is Total Distance.
In
Seat Belt Score,
Formula can contain only numbers, variables ''e'' and ''t'' and following symbols : +, -, /, *, (, ).  you can click on
to see a preview of how the score will function.
Eg:-  e , e+t , e+2 , e-2*t.
Variable "e" is Seat Belt Duration & Variable "t" is Total Distance.
In
Total Score,
You can configure how the total score for the R.A.G should be calculated, Formula can contain only numbers, variables ''f'', "g", "h", "i" and "j" and following symbols : +, -, /, *, (, ).  you can click on
to see a preview of how the score will function.
Eg:- j+i+h+g+f*2.
Variable "f" is Harsh Acceleration Score , Variable "g" is Harsh Breaking Score , Variable "h" is Harsh Cornering Score , Variable "i" is Overspeed Score , Variable "j" is Seat Belt Score.
In
Threshold
, you can set the score limits for
Green
,
Amber
, and
Red
. Based on the
total score
, the driver will be categorized under the corresponding color
Click on the
Save 💾 icon
to save the configuration.
To download the created RAG configuration go on the overview page and click on
icon to download excel format,

Title: How to create a Customized API on the platform?
URL: https://helpdesk.uffizio.com/knowledge/customized-api

How to create a Customized API on the platform?
An API (Application Programming Interface) serves as a bridge that allows different software applications to interact and exchange data effectively.
A customized API empowers users to access and retrieve report data available on the platform, facilitating seamless sharing with third-party applications.
This document explains how to configure and use the customized API module in our software.
Please Note:
The User Customize API feature is available only to users with the Premium version of the platform.
Watch :
how to configure user customize API.
To Get Started
Log in to your account.
Go to
Settings > Master > User Customize API.
Click on the
+
button
.
Choose the report name from the
API Category
list that corresponds to the data you wish to share.
Enter
API Name.
Select
Timezone
from the list: The data will be shared according to the selected timezone.
Enter
Frequency Time
.
The minimum interval for making requests is set at 2 minutes per call. This means that after a request is made, you must wait at least 2 minutes before initiating the next request.
Select
Response Type
.
Select the
Pull Request Parameters
Type/Format according to your requirements.
Select
Start Date Time
format from the predefined list.
Select
End Date
Time
format from the predefined list.
The default format for
IMEI Numbers
is String.
Choose the
Output Data
fields you wish to include by checking the corresponding checkboxes next to each field name.
Enter a custom field name in the
Rename As
column next to the fields you have selected, based on your specific requirements.
Choose the appropriate
Type / Format
from the options available next to the fields you have selected, tailored to meet your specific needs.
The changes after you add the fields would be visible in the
Request Body Preview
and
Response Body Preview
.
Click on the
Save 💾
icon to save the configuration.
To Test the API
Go to
Settings > Master > User Customize API.
Click on the
Orange Dot
in the
Test API
column of the API that needs to be tested.
A dialog box will appear, prompting you to enter the parameter values for the Test API request.
Enter
Start Date Time.
Enter
End Date
Time
.
Enter
IMEI
Numbers
.
Please Note:
For APIs that require both a
Start Date and an End Date
, please be aware that the
maximum allowable date range
for selection is
10 days
.
Click on
Test
to test the API.
Below is a description of the various color-coded Test API dots you will encounter on the Overview screen, along with their corresponding meanings:
Orange:
The test is pending and has not yet been conducted.
Green:
The test is successful.
Red:
The test has failed due to a specific reason, which you can identify by hovering over the dot for further details.
To Integrate the API
Please Note:
The User Customized API is designed to be accessible by all users under the admin account. To use the API, you must first generate a token specific to your user account. Once the token is generated, it enables access to the API for retrieving data related to the vehicles associated with the user account for which the token was created.
Step 1:
Generate a token for the specific user account.
Step 2:
Use the generated token in the header to access the configured API and retrieve the required data.

Title: Edit Admin Account
URL: https://helpdesk.uffizio.com/knowledge/smartbus/edit-admin-account

Edit Admin Account
The Admin oversees the platform's functionality, which includes creating users, assigning roles, and managing permissions.
Admin account will be created by the super admin and handed over to the designated user. Users will be able to make changes and update the admin account according to their needs.
To Get Started
Log in to your
Admin
account.
Go to

Change Account Password
Learn how to change the account password easily. There are two ways to change the password. Both ways are given below.
Please Note:-
The process given here is an example for Admin Account but If you want to Change the Password of any other account such as a
sub-user Reseller or School
the
process will remain same, only the Account will change from Admin to the other account.
If you are not able to change the password then, contact your admin.
Option 1:
Login to your account.
Go to
Settings > General > Admin/ Reseller/ School
.
Double-click on the account you want to change the password.
Navigate to
My Account
.
Click on
Change Password
.
Enter your
Old password
below that enter
New Password > Retype Password.
Click on the
Save 💾 icon
.
Now you can use your new password for the next login.
Please Note:-
-Password must be of at least 8 characters.
-Password must contain at least one uppercase character (A-Z),
one lowercase character (a-z), and one digit (0-9) and special characters from (!,@,#,$,%,&,*,?).
Option 2:
Login to your account.
On the
Left-side Menu
below the logo find
User
.
Click on
User
> Change Password
.
Enter your
Old password
below that enter
New Password > Retype  Password
.

Save 💾 icon
.

Title: Reset Password
URL: https://helpdesk.uffizio.com/knowledge/smartbus/reset-password

Reset Password
The system allows the user to Reset their login password in case the user is unable to recall the password. This guide outlines the steps required to reset a new password.
The same steps need to be followed to reset the password for the Admin / Reseller/ Company account.
Before You Get Started
Please Note:
Email configuration
on the particular user
(Admin / Reseller/ Company) or its parent user is required to receive email for
Password Reset Link.
To successfully receive the password reset link, please verify that the email address linked to the user account is correctly entered in the
Password Recovery Email
field located in the My Account tab of your user configuration.
You can reset it from the
Login page
by clicking
Forgot my password.
You will be asked to enter the
Username
of your account.
An email will be sent to you with a link and instructions for resetting your password.
Click on the
link
given.
It will redirect you to a password reset page.
Enter a new password and retype it in the box below.
Please Note:
Password must be of at least 8 characters.
Password must contain at least one uppercase character (A-Z), one lowercase character (a-z) and one digit (0-9) and special characters from (!,@,#,$,%,&,*,?).
Click on the
Update Password
button.
Now you can use your new password and log in to the account again.

Title: Map Configuration for Admin Account
URL: https://helpdesk.uffizio.com/knowledge/smartbus/map-configuration-for-admin-account

Map Configuration for Admin Account
The system enables the user to configure the map according to their specific needs, which can significantly enhance the experience of live fleet tracking.
Please Note:
AWe currently provide a range of map services designed to enhance fleet tracking efficiency. The OSM map is a default map provided in the system.
Before You Get Started
According to your requirement, if you require a map service other than OSM, you will need to purchase a map key from your chosen service provider.
Below is a list of the map services that we have integrated into our system.
Bing
Geofusion
GOOGLE
HERE
HERE_CUSTOM
HERE_V8
HEREv2
LocationIQ
Map My India
Mapbox
Navionics
NORGESKART
ORM
OSM
TOMTOM
Yandex
After purchasing the service, you will receive a Web Map API Key, a Mobile Map API Key, and a Project ID from your service provider. Please note that these credentials may vary depending on the map provider and are essential for configuring the selected map within the application.
To Get Started
Log in to your account.
Go to
Settings > General > Admin.
Double-click on the account for which you want to set the map.
Navigate to
Map.
To Configure Map
Click on
Add New
a new row appears.
Choose the
Map
from the drop-down menu for which the API services you have purchased.
Input the
Web Map API Key
received by your service provider to access the various features of the map on the web platform.
If your map provider offers a separate Mobile Map API Key, please enter it in the
Mobile Map Key
section to enable access to the map features specifically designed for your mobile application.
Enter the
Map Project ID
if it is received from your chosen map service provider.
Please Note:
Not all Map service providers provide a Map Project ID, and its availability may differ between providers.
You can also configure other features from the
Configuration
option.
Snap to Road :
This feature can be used for aligning a GPS point to the nearest point on a road network.
Address From Map Provider
: If enabled, the system will request and display the location address through the Map Provider's "Reverse Geocoding" service for the coordinates received from the device.
Please Note:
To use this feature, "Geocoding API" should be enabled in the Map API Key.
Speed Limit API:
By enabling this API, the system can get the speed limit for a specific location or road. Utilizing this service, the system can generate an Overspeed alert based on the specific speed limit of the road.
Please Note:
The "Speed Limit API" should be enabled in the Map API Key to utilize this feature.
Street View:
This feature allows users to view their fleet from a street-level perspective on the map, as long as the chosen map service provider offers street view functionality and the relevant street view data is accessible for the given location.
Please Note:
To utilize this feature, the "Street View API" should be enabled in the Map API Key.
Default:
The default option is beneficial for fleet owners who utilize multiple maps, as it allows them to make a single map as the primary one for their operations.
For example,
A fleet owner can set OSM as the default map.
A fleet owner can use the HERE map for speed limit API.
A fleet owner can use Google Maps for identifying addresses.
Click on the
Save 💾
icon.
Please Note:
The map will be displayed on the live tracking screen on the web and mobile application, and additional related details will be available in the reports.

Title: SMS Service Configuration
URL: https://helpdesk.uffizio.com/knowledge/smartbus/sms-service-configuration

SMS Service Configuration
The system provides the feature to set up an SMS service that delivers alert information directly to users' mobile numbers.
SMS configuration can be done in an Admin account, resellers as well as school users can inherit the configuration. SMS is one of the most effective channels for sending alerts.
Before You Get Started
You need to purchase a third-party Bulk SMS service from a service provider that meets your requirements from the below Options:
GET
POST
In SMS configuration, the
GET
and
POST
methods are two ways to interact with SMS gateways via APIs. They serve to initiate and manage SMS sending by sending requests to an SMS provider’s API.
To Get Started
Log in to your account.
Go to
Settings > General > Admin.
Double-click on the account for which you want to configure SMS.
Navigate to
SMS.
To Configure SMS
SMS Gateway
field will be Custom by default.
Select the
Gateway Type
, either
GET
or
POST
.
GET
method is used when data is requested from a specified resource. To send a GET request, a client needs to specify the URL of the resource it wants to retrieve. Your SMS service provider would be providing the details, which you will have to enter in the mentioned field.
In the
SMS Gateway URL
field, please input the API URL provided by your SMS service provider into the designated text box.
Refer to the
Example
to check the kind of URL you will receive.
Variable
parameters must be specified in the SMS API URL as illustrated in the example. This allows the software to retrieve the mobile number you have provided in the alert configuration and generate the corresponding message alerts accordingly.
Please Note:
The "TemplateId" is an optional variable that may be utilized depending on your API configuration. If your SMS API requires TemplateId, you will need to specify it accordingly when setting up your SMS configuration.
POST
method is used to send data to a server to create/update a resource. The data sent to the server with POST is stored in the request body of the HTTP request.
Select
Gateway Vendor
from the predefined list.
Please fill in the necessary details in the fields that are displayed after selecting your chosen vendor. This information should be obtained from a service provider.
Click on the
Save 💾 icon.

Title: Email Service Configuration
URL: https://helpdesk.uffizio.com/knowledge/smartbus/email-service-configuration

Email Service Configuration
The system allows you to configure Email Service to send alerts and reports directly to users via email. Admin can set up the Email configuration on their account, and it will automatically be inherited by Resellers and Company users if they have not set up their own Email configurations.
Before You Get Started
Purchase the Bulk Email service from a service provider that meets your needs, selecting from one of the options below:
SMTP
: SMTP is a protocol specifically designed for sending and relaying emails between servers or from a client to a server.
POST:
The POST method is a general HTTP request method used to send data from a client to a server over the web. It is commonly used in web forms and APIs, including some web-based email services.
To Get Started
Log in to your account.
Go to
Settings > General > Admin
.
Double-click on the account for which you want to configure email service.
Navigate to
Email
tab.
To Configure Email Service
Choose the appropriate method that matches the email configuration you have purchased from the available options.
SMTP /
POST
For SMTP Method :
In
From
Email Address,
enter the email address that will be used to send emails through the software.
Enter
Username, Password, Host, and Outgoing Port
provided by your service provider.
To enable
SMTP
Authentication
click on the checkbox given.
SMTP Authentication
ensures that only authorized users can send emails through the server, enhancing security and deliverability. Please verify with your Email Service Provider that this feature is enabled before selecting the same.
To enable
TLS Authentication
click on the checkbox given.
TLS (Transport Layer Security)
is a protocol that encrypts data transmitted over the internet for secure communication. Ensure this feature is activated by your Email Service Provider before enabling it.
To enable
Email Verification
, check the provided checkbox. This feature ensures that the system sends a verification email to the recipient. Only after the recipient confirms their email address, the system will be authorized to send additional emails.
Click on the
Test configuration
button to test if the configuration is working.
Upon clicking on Test Configuration, below popup window will appear.
Enter any valid email address in the text box given.
Click on the
Verify
button.
A verification email would be sent to the test email ID mentioning “Your email verification is successful.”  Also, a verification message will pop up on the screen.
Please Note:
In case of a wrong email ID or incomplete email ID, an error message will be displayed.
Click on the
Save 💾
icon.
For Post Method:
Select the
Gateway vendor
from the predefined list.
Please provide the necessary information in the fields that will be displayed after selecting the vendor. You should acquire these details from your service provider.
Please Note:
Currently, we have integrated "Twilio" as our primary Gateway vendor; however, if you want to use any other gateway, we are open to incorporating it into our platform; contact us for further details.
To enable
Email Verification
, check the provided checkbox. This feature ensures that the system sends a verification email to the recipient. Only after the recipient confirms their email address will the system be authorized to send additional emails.
Click on the
Test configuration
button to test if the configuration is working.
Upon clicking on Test Configuration, the below popup window will appear.
Enter any valid email address in the text box given.
Click on the
Verify
button.
A verification email would be sent to the test email ID mentioning “Your email verification is successful.”  Also, a verification message will pop up on the screen.
Please Note:
In case of a wrong email ID or incomplete email ID, an error message will be displayed.
Click on the
Save 💾
icon.

Right Side
of the
Name
field for drafting the Email message.

Location Alert- Your vehicle %plateno% with current speed %speed% on %datetime% is at %location%.

Default
field to enter the message.

on the

Add New

and the Admin Subuser window will open.

If the
Map
API key is configured on Admin account and you want to specify which map service would be given access to the sub-user, then you can choose the option from the drop-down list.
Note :
The map field and option will only be available if map details are added at your end.
Choose the preferred
Language
from the drop-down list. This selection will determine the language in which the admin sub-user will access the data.
If you want to have the cover page (Title Page) when you download the reports, then click on the checkbox to enable
Show Cover Page on Download.
Contact Detail Masking:
If you do not want to show the parent mobile number or email to the subuser, you can mask it by choosing the appropriate option from
Select Parameter for Masking
drop-down.
Please Note:
The sub-user will have access to analytics for the selected objects only, according to the screen rights assigned to them.
Save
the settings by clicking on the
Save 💾 icon.

Custom
by default.

and

: To use the IVR configuration from the parent user.
Custom
: To configure a unique IVR service specific to their account.

field, select the preferred IVR service gateway, which is currently set to
Twilio
, as it is the default integration on the system.
Enter
Account SID
received from your service provider.
Enter
Account
Token
in the given field.

From Number
field, enter the phone number you want the call to be made from.

Save 💾 icon
.

Manage Authentication for Admin

Authentication Tab
is integrated into the platform to provide an extra layer of security through two-step verification (2FA). This feature is crucial for safeguarding user accounts and sensitive actions like login by requiring OTP (One-Time Password) verification.

Go to
Settings > General > Admin
Double-click on the admin record for which you want to authenticate the user.

User Login
Authentication
Select the
Authentication Required For
.
Select from the options mentioned to
Provide Verification Medium
by which the OTP will be received for verification.
Two-step authentication (2FA)
for logging into the platform is achieved through OTPs sent via SMS or email, or by using Authenticator apps like Google Authenticator, Authy, or Chrome’s Authenticator extension.
Click on
Verify
after completing the process mentioned in the above image.
Click on
Save 💾
button.
For
Announcement
Authentication
Select the
Authentication Required For
.
Enter the
Mobile Number
for receiving the OTP for verification purposes and click on
Verify
to verify the mobile number
.
Enter the
Email
for receiving the OTP for verification purposes and click on
Verify
to verify the email
.
Click on
Save 💾
button.
You can also select both the
Authentication Required For
options if needed. Follow the steps to fill in the details respectively and click on Save.

Title: SSO (Single Sign On)
URL: https://helpdesk.uffizio.com/knowledge/smartbus/single-sign-on

SSO (Single Sign On)
The
SSO (Single Sign-On) functionality enables users to authenticate using their existing credentials from third-party identity providers like Google, Microsoft, or other supported systems.
This feature streamlines the login process by allowing users to log in using credentials from their organization's identity provider. It enhances security by reducing the need for managing multiple passwords and delivers a more efficient and user-friendly experience.
Supported Providers
: The system initially supports OAuth 2.0, OpenID Connect, and SAML-based providers such as Google, Microsoft Azure AD, and Okta.
To Get Started
Log in to your account.
Go to
Settings > General > Admin/Reseller/Company.
Double-click on the account for which you want to configure the SSO.
Navigate to
SSO.
To Configure SSO
Click on
Add New,
and a popup to configure SSO will appear.
Initially, we have integrated Azure and OKTA for SSO configuration.
For Azure or Okta, select the desired provider and enter the required details, such as Client ID, Client Secret, and other necessary credentials provided by the respective provider.
Click on the Save
💾
icon to save the configuration.
To Login with SSO
On the login screen, you will get an option for Single Sign-On.
Click on SSO and you will be redirected to the SSO login page
Select your preferred provider and enter the username.
Click on Login, and you will be redirected to that provider's sign-in page.
Enter the username and password on your provider's sign-in page, and after a successful login, you will be landed on the startup screen of the smart bus platform.

Title: Web and Mobile Access For Subuser
URL: https://helpdesk.uffizio.com/knowledge/smartbus/web-and-mobile-access-for-sub-user

Web and Mobile Access For Subuser
Admin users have the ability to set up Web and Mobile access for their sub-users. These rights enable the sub-user to access the platform through a web portal or mobile application.
Please Note:
Here we have shown the steps to be followed for Admin Subuser. Same procedure should be followed in the case of Reseller sub-users and Company Subuser.
To Get Started
Log in to your account.
Go to
Settings > General > Admin.
Double-click on the account for which you want to set up web or mobile access.
Navigate to the
Admin Subuser
tab.
Click on
Add New.
Navigate to
User settings.
To Provide Web Access
Click
on
All
if you want the sub-user to provide
Web platform
access.
Click
on
None
if you don’t want the sub-user to access the Web platform.
Click
on
Specific
if you want the sub-user to have a web platform via a specific IP address.
After selecting Specific, please enter the permitted
IP Address
in the designated text box. You can enter multiple IP commas separated.
To Provide Mobile Access
Click
on
All
if you want the sub-user to have
Mobile Application
access
.
Click
on
None
if you don’t want the sub-user to access the Mobile application.
Click
on
Specific
if you want the sub-user to have access to the Mobile application with a specific mobile or IP address.
Click
on
Unique ID
if you want the sub-user to have access to the Mobile application via a specific mobile device only.
After selecting Unique ID, you will be asked to enter the
Mobile Unique Identification Number
.
Please locate the
Unique Id
on the sign-in page of the mobile application installed on your phone and enter it in the designated text box provided. You can enter multiple IP addresses separated by commas.
Click
on
IP Address
if you want the sub-user to have Mobile application access via a specific IP address.
You will be asked to enter
IP Address;
provide the permitted IP addresses in the text box provided. You can enter multiple IP addresses separated by commas.
Save the configuration by clicking on the
Save 💾 icon.

Title: Create a Reseller Account
URL: https://helpdesk.uffizio.com/knowledge/smartbus/crease-a-reseller-account

Create a Reseller Account
A
Reseller
is a business or individual that purchases software or services from a distributor or provider and then sells them to end customers.
In the system, Reseller purchases the software from the Admin and subsequently sells it to their end customers, offering personalized branding and pricing options. The Admin has the ability to create multiple reseller accounts based on their specific needs.
This document provides a step-by-step guide on how to create a new reseller account.
To Get Started
Log in to your
Admin
account.
Go to
Settings > General > Reseller.
Click
on the
➕
icon on the taskbar below.
To Create a Reseller Account
Navigate to
My Account
Select the
Country
from the drop-down menu.
Select the
State
from the drop-down menu.
Add a
Short Name
for the reseller.
Add a
User Name
for the reseller. Use an email address as a user name.
Confirm the User Name
by entering it again.
Click on the checkbox for
Email Login Details
to mail the created login credentials to the reseller.
Please Note:
Email configuration should be set on Admin user to mail the login credentials to Reseller. Learn how to
Setup Email Configuration.
Add a
Password
for Reseller account.
Retype the Password.
Please Note:
Password must be of at least 8 characters.
Password must contain at least one uppercase character (A-Z), one lowercase character (a-z), and one digit (0-9) and special characters from (!,@,#,$,%,&,*,?).
You can set a
Security Pin
for the reseller.
Enter the
Password Recovery Email
address on which the password reset link will be sent while performing
Reset password.
Enter Address details like
City, Zip code, Street1, Street2
etc.
Enter the concerned person name in
Contact Person
for whom the user is being created.
You can easily upload a
Logo
for the reseller.
Enter
Helpdesk Details.
Enter
Fax Number.
Enter a
Welcome Message
which will be displayed on the startup screen upon user login.
Enter
GSTIN
number of the reseller's organization.
Enter
PAN No
number of the reseller's organization.
Define the duration of
Data Storage
for the reseller. This period determines the number of days the reseller can access and analyze data on the platform. For example, if set to 90 days, the reseller will have access to analytics for the past 90 days.
Please Note:
Data Storage will be for 90 days by default. If you want to increase the number of days, contact your admin.
Navigate to Rule
Learn how the Admin can
Create a new Rule
for their resellers according to their customized requirements.
Navigate to User Settings
The User Settings section in the Reseller account enables users to customize their preferences according to their specific needs for various platform features.
Enter the preferred
Time Zone
from the predefined options. The chosen timezone will be utilized to present analytics for the reseller account within the application.
You can edit
Date and Time
format.
Select the
Week Start Day.
The application will produce weekly reports based on the start day of the week that has been configured on your reseller account.
Choose the
User Status
to determine the current state of the user's account. This setting allows you to activate or deactivate the account, controlling the user access as needed.
Show Default Filter Option:
You can turn on/off the "Records per page" drop-down being displayed on the bottom right of all the screens on the platform.
Select the
Show Object Name On Report
checkbox if you wish to display the object name on the report.

option.
Forcefully First Login

By selecting this option, you can set the condition for the user to change the password for their account when they logs into the account for the first time.
If you want to grant vehicle

rights to the user, then select the provided checkbox.

: If this option is enabled, the vehicle will be immobilized if an unauthorized person attempts to move it while it is in parking mode. (Note: The Immobilization sensor port must be configured on the object.)
Select the checkbox for enabling the

for the reseller account. This ensures the Installation Date field is required when adding a vehicle under that reseller. The field will be available in the Profile tab of the Vehicle module.

Title: Device Accuracy Tolerance For Reseller
URL: https://helpdesk.uffizio.com/knowledge/smartbus/device-accuracy-tolerance-for-reseller

Device Accuracy Tolerance For Reseller
Admin can set up device accuracy tolerance for the objects under reseller account.
Device Accuracy Tolerance will ignore the data if the device data received from the device is drifting within the default radius of 20 meters.
To get started
Login to the admin account
Go to
Settings > General > Reseller
Double-click on the reseller account for which you want to set the device accuracy tolerance.
Navigate to
Rule
. A new window named
Reseller Rule
will open.
After entering the rule name, description, and date of the rule.
In the
Device Accuracy Tolerance
enter the radius for which you want the device data to be ignored.
Please Note:-
By default we provide a 20-meter radius as the device accuracy tolerance.
Click on
Save icon.
